### 1. 超写实网球美学团体照提示词

**作者**: [glena Jenner](https://x.com/GlenaJenne/status/2041266373205344468)  **日期**: 2026-04-06  **语言**: en

> 这是一份高度详细且结构化的提示词，用于生成一张在户外网球场上拍摄的四位特定女性主体的超写实团体照。重点在于对称构图、强烈的自然日光，以及从上传的参考图中精确保留人物特征。

![超写实网球美学团体照提示词](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1775544742520_t30rtd_HFQI8EaawAA1MdG.jpg)

```
{
  "scene": {
    "setting": "outdoor tennis court",
    "background": "clean blue tennis court with white lines, net in center, green trees and fencing in background, clear bright blue sky with minimal clouds, open sunny environment",
    "lighting": "strong natural daylight with realistic sun direction, bright highlights and defined shadows, natural reflections on court surface, balanced exposure with no overexposure"
  },
  "subject": {
    "type": "group of four females",
    "pose": "two women standing behind the tennis net with relaxed confident posture, two women kneeling in front of the net on the court with legs folded to the side, all positioned symmetrically like reference composition",
    "expression": "confident and relaxed expressions with subtle smiles, natural gaze toward camera",
    "face": "Use uploaded reference image, keep identity exact for each subject, natural facial structure with realistic skin texture, visible pores and minor imperfections, accurate lighting interaction",
    "hair": "Use uploaded reference image, keep identity exact for each subject, natural hair color and style with realistic volume and movement",
    "eyes": "Use uploaded reference image, keep identity exact, clearly visible eyes, no sunglasses",
    "skin": "natural sunlit skin tones with realistic texture, subtle highlights and shadows, no smoothing"
  },
  "clothing": {
    "outfits": "tennis-style dresses in soft pastel tones including {argument name="outfit color 1" default="white"}, {argument name="outfit color 2" default="light blue"}, and {argument name="outfit color 3" default="pink"}, fitted athletic design with pleated skirts, lightweight fabric with natural folds and movement",
    "footwear": "white athletic tennis shoes with realistic detail and slight court contact",
    "accessories": "tennis rackets and balls, minimal jewelry, no sunglasses"
  },
  "environment_details": {
    "props": "tennis net, rackets placed on court, tennis balls scattered naturally",
    "textures": "court surface texture, fabric pleats, natural skin detail, subtle wear on equipment"
  },
  "camera": {
    "angle": "low to eye-level angle centered on group",
    "framing": "full group shot with symmetrical composition and net dividing scene",
    "focus": "sharp focus on all subjects with slight background blur",
    "lens": "wide-angle lens with natural perspective"
  },
  "style": {
    "realism": "ultra realistic",
    "color_tone": "bright natural tones with strong blue sky contrast and soft pastel outfit colors",
    "effects": "subtle HDR, natural contrast, realistic color grading, no artificial filters",
    "details": "high detail textures, accurate lighting interaction, realistic shadows, no over-processing"
  }
}
```

Left: woman in a light blue police uniform with cap, making an “OK” gesture near her eye with a playful expression.

Bottom right: woman dressed as a nurse in a white outfit and cap, making a peace (V) sign with a cute expression.

### 8. iPhone 户外自然光摄影

**作者**: [glena Jenner](https://x.com/GlenaJenne/status/2040087637571367071)  **日期**: 2026-04-03  **语言**: en

> 一个高度结构化的 JSON 提示词，用于生成一张由 iPhone 17 Pro 拍摄的超写实、抓拍风格户外照片。该提示词强调保留参考图像中的精确面部特征、强烈的自然阳光，以及在阳光明媚的路边场景中呈现真实、随意的生活方式美感。

![iPhone 户外自然光摄影](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1775284639562_4f5g5m_HE_Y4LbasAEupDO.jpg)
![iPhone 户外自然光摄影](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1775284639634_pc6o4l_HE_Y3daaEAAjB6Z.jpg)
![iPhone 户外自然光摄影](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1775284639774_tzhg4h_HE_Y40jaUAAhP2q.jpg)

```
{
  "meta": {
    "camera": "iPhone 17 Pro",
    "lens": "24mm wide",
    "aspect_ratio": "9:16",
    "quality": "ultra photorealistic, 8K, HDR",
    "style": "iphone outdoor photography, natural sunlight, slight grain, real-life candid look"
  },

  "subject": {
    "identity": "use reference image face",
    "identity_lock": "strictly preserve exact facial features, proportions, skin tone, eye color, and hair color from reference image, no changes",

    "expression": "natural smile, friendly, relaxed confidence",
    
    "skin": "realistic skin texture, visible pores, slight sun highlights, no over-smoothing",
    
    "hair": {
      "style": "soft natural waves",
      "behavior": "slight movement from outdoor breeze, realistic strands"
    },

    "body": {
      "type": "natural proportions",
      "details": "relaxed posture, realistic anatomy"
    }
  },

  "scene": {
    "location": "sunny roadside with palm trees",
    "environment": "open street, light traffic, tropical vibe, clear blue sky with clouds",
    "details": "restaurant-style outdoor setting, signboard in background, casual environment",
    "atmosphere": "bright, warm, everyday real-life moment"
  },

  "lighting": {
    "main": "direct sunlight",
    "effect": "strong highlights, natural shadows, slightly harsh contrast, realistic outdoor exposure"
  },

  "camera": {
    "perspective": "casual iphone shot",
    "angle": "eye-level slightly tilted",
    "framing": "mid-body shot",
    "imperfection": "slight overexposure in highlights, natural shadow fall, handheld feel"
  },

  "pose": {
    "body": "standing relaxed",
    "arms": "one hand resting on hip, other hanging naturally",
    "head": "slightly tilted with direct gaze"
  },

  "outfit": {
    "top": "fitted white long-sleeve top with logo detail",
    "bottom": "bright orange shorts",
    "details": "clean, sporty casual look"
  },

  "vibe": {
    "energy": "friendly, confident, approachable",
    "mood": "sunny day, casual lifestyle",
    "realism": "feels like a real outdoor photo taken on iphone"
  }
}
```

### 11. Sabrina Carpenter 风格酒店走廊照片

**作者**: [babydoll](https://x.com/bananababydoll/status/2039346295069126730)  **日期**: 2026-04-01  **语言**: en

> 一份为 Google Nano Banana Pro 准备的详细 JSON 提示词，旨在生成一张以 Sabrina Carpenter 为灵感、极具超写实感的酒店走廊夜间抓拍照片，重点强调 iPhone 闪光灯照明、高对比度以及关于她外貌和穿搭的具体细节。

![Sabrina Carpenter 风格酒店走廊照片](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1775112281907_w9nbyf_HEadmjrWYAAzd5C.jpg)

```
{
  "meta": {
    "camera": "iPhone 17 Pro",
    "lens": "24mm wide",
    "aspect_ratio": "9:16",
    "quality": "ultra photorealistic",
    "style": "iphone flash photo, slight grain, high contrast highlights"
  },

  "subject": {
    "identity": "{argument name="celebrity identity" default="sabrina carpenter inspired"}",
    "face": {
      "structure": "petite heart-shaped face, full lips, soft cheeks",
      "skin": "fair warm tone, visible pores, subtle gloss highlights",
      "expression": "playful but controlled, lips slightly parted, confident gaze"
    },
    "hair": {
      "color": "golden blonde",
      "style": "soft voluminous waves, slightly messy texture"
    },
    "body": {
      "type": "petite curvy",
      "waist": "very slim",
      "hips": "round",
      "chest": "full and natural"
    }
  },

  "scene": {
    "location": "luxury hotel hallway",
    "time": "2:11 AM",
    "atmosphere": "post-party silence, warm dim lights"
  },

  "lighting": {
    "main": "iphone flash",
    "secondary": "warm hallway ambient lights",
    "effect": "hard highlights on skin, deep shadows behind, glossy skin reflections"
  },

  "camera": {
    "perspective": "third-person candid",
    "angle": "slightly low",
    "distance": "mid body",
    "imperfection": "slight blur, imperfect framing"
  },

  "pose": {
    "body": "hips slightly pushed back, torso angled",
    "legs": "one knee bent",
    "head": "tilted slightly down while eyes look up"
  },

**作者**: [hxhxhx0916](https://x.com/hxhxhx0916/status/2038944899895353471)  **日期**: 2026-03-31  **语言**: zh

> 一份为 Nano Banana Pro 设计的详细结构化提示词，用于生成超写实的商业时尚摄影作品。场景描绘了一个角色躺在装满液体的巨大鸡尾酒杯中，强调真实的皮肤纹理、优雅的姿态、动态的溅射效果、电影级光影以及高分辨率。需要提供一张角色面部和头发的参考照片。

![适用于 Nano Banana Pro 的超写实商业时尚摄影提示词](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1775026357959_5676s1_HEvJR2EbAAA-nDE.jpg)

```
角色躺在装满饮料的巨型鸡尾酒杯中的超写实摄影棚照片。使用[角色照片]作为面部和头发的精确参考，保持自然的皮肤纹理、毛孔和真实的身体比例。俯拍角度，全身可见，手臂和腿部放松且姿态优雅，部分浸入饮料表面，周围环绕着动态的奶油状飞溅和水滴。湿润的皮肤和闪亮的高光，仿佛被饮料覆盖。高端时尚造型，戏剧性的电影级灯光，玻璃杯上强烈的阴影和反射，光泽高光，8K分辨率，极其清晰的焦点，超高细节，照片级写实，无失真，无多余人物，无文字，无水印。
```

### 21. 身份一致性连拍模拟

**作者**: [Mr Das](https://x.com/MrDasOnX/status/2037396204146081806)  **日期**: 2026-03-27  **语言**: en

> 一个高度详细、结构化的提示词，旨在生成一张超现实的竖版照片，模拟智能手机连拍效果，确保在三个堆叠的帧中，脸部身份保持完美一致，同时描绘一个身穿特定服装、位于特定地点的男性，并带有自然的瑕疵。

![身份一致性连拍模拟](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1774679867387_vquntd_HEZJCzDa8AA8Wk1.jpg)

```
Use the uploaded reference photo as the only facial identity reference.
The same exact face must appear in all three frames.
Do not change identity, do not beautify, do not stylize, do not reinterpret the face.
Facial identity must stay perfectly consistent across all frames.

Ultra-realistic vertical photo divided into three equal stacked frames inside one single image.
All three frames show the same man, same clothes, same location, captured seconds apart like a casual smartphone burst photo.
Natural imperfections allowed. Slight motion blur allowed. Identity must stay identical.

Location:
Outdoor sidewalk in daylight.
White plaster wall with Bougainvillea glabra climbing plants.
Natural urban background, realistic, not staged.

Outfit (locked):
Pastel yellow loose button-down shirt, top buttons open, sleeves rolled to forearms, untucked.
Off-white straight fit trousers.
Metal wristwatch.
No sunglasses.

Hair & face (locked):
Medium length wavy messy hair.
Natural skin texture, visible pores.
No beauty filter, no smoothing.

TOP FRAME:
Back angled shot, turning away.
Hand running through back of hair near neck.
Face mostly hidden.
Slight motion blur on hand and hair.
Casual, unposed, Gen-Z energy.

MIDDLE FRAME:
Close-up of upper face.
Hair falling across forehead covering one eye.
Eyes half visible, looking sideways/down.
Soft focus, slight motion softness.
Feels accidental, intimate.

BOTTOM FRAME:
Mid shot.
Leaning casually against wall.
One hand near pocket or adjusting cuff.
Looking away from camera.
Relaxed, natural posture.

Lighting:
Natural daylight, soft shadows, realistic phone camera look.
Not cinematic, not studio, not HDR.

Style:
Ultra realistic
smartphone photo
burst shot
imperfect framing
human, casual, real
identity locked
same person all frames
```

**Related**: [[超现实]]、[[宠物]]

### 26. Bat Cowl Protocol 角色提示

**作者**: [Edizkan ⭕🦇](https://x.com/edizkan_/status/2036444796965835075)  **日期**: 2026-03-24  **语言**: en

> 一个复杂的提示，用于让 Nano Banana（或 Gemini Nano Banana）生成一个高质量的 设计师玩具角色 3D 渲染图，同时将 参考图片 中的一个定制 'Bat Cowl' 整合到该角色上，并严格保持该角色原有的服装、形象和光照条件。

![Bat Cowl Protocol 角色提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1774421473775_ksdvy8_HELkjkWaIAEqNjn.jpg)

```
A high-quality 3D render of the designer toy from [Reference Image 1]. Requirement: The character must retain its exact original outfit . The Mask: Tightly fit a custom "Bat Cowl" ([Reference Image 2]) over the head.

The Cowl: Must match the exact color, material, and design, with size adjusted as needed to fit the reference character’s head.
Scaling: Tailored, bespoke fit with a shortened chin guard precisely following the character's jawline. Cowl size is adjusted to match the reference character exactly. The cowl fits seamlessly, with no gap between the head and the chin guard.
Ears: Only the sharp bat ears are visible; hide original ears, headwears, horn, accessories, hat, helmet entirely.
The Cutout: The cowl features a cutout area; through this opening, the underlying part of the reference character must be visible exactly as it is, with no additions, removals, or alterations.
Eyes: Use the exact glowing eye effect from the reference cowl image.
Constraint: No nose or eyes should be rendered on the cowl or the character's face.
8k, studio lighting, Background must match the reference character’s background exactly.
Lighting
Lighting should match the reference character’s original light behavior, and the cowl must follow and respond to the same lighting conditions.
Character Likeness Integrity (CRITICAL)

Maintain the exact eye shape, spacing, stylization, patterns, silhouette, and original color palette from the reference.

Do not humanize.

Do not alter anatomy.

Do not modify facial structure.

Identity must remain instantly recognizable.

If the character wears a balaclava, mask, helmet, or covered face, don't invent facial anatomy.
No added nose.

No added mouth.

No visible skin where the reference does not show it.
```

**Related**: [[3D渲染]]、[[综合3D]]、[[综合动漫]]

> 一个高度结构化的 JSON 提示，用于 Nano Banana Pro 生成一个以 Disney-Pixar 风格呈现的 Blackpink 成员 Rosé 的 3D 动画角色模型。它指定了超高清渲染（8k，Octane/Unreal Engine 5 风格）、详细的服装纹理（淡紫色短款连帽衫和工装慢跑裤）、柔和的影棚灯光，以及以无缝灰色背景为衬托的全身居中构图。

"lighting": "Soft, diffused studio lighting setup. Features a gentle key light to warmly illuminate her face and outfit, a subtle fill light to soften any harsh shadows, and a crisp rim light catching the edges of her blonde hair to separate her beautifully from the grey background.",

![韩式网红风格自拍提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1772519715378_ewiehq_HCY8t5MaUAA9zn2.jpg)

```
Create A Close-up selfie of a beautiful young woman.
Skin: Porcelain white, bright, smooth, and poreless.
Face: Symmetrical; do not change the original face.
Style: Edgy and mysterious.
Pose: Standing in a room (likely a living room). Head tilted down, looking towards the camera. Calm expression with lips slightly parted, biting the index finger.
Camera Angle: Low angle selfie.
Outfit & Accessories:
Outfit:  reference photo 2.
Accessories: Small thin necklace with a rose pendant; medium-sized hoop earrings.
Nails: Light brown with white tips (French tip style).
Makeup (Detailed Korean Ulzzang Style):
Skin Finish: Super smooth glass skin, milky bright tone, thin dewy glowing foundation.
Highlighting: Soft highlights on the forehead, nose, and chin.
Eyebrows: Straight,tebal  natural, soft,.
Eye Makeup: Soft pink-peach gradient with subtle shimmer; very thin "puppy" eyeliner; long, curly, naturally separated eyelashes.
Under-eye: Clear and glowing "aegyo sal" with small highlights; brightened under-eye area.
Blush: Baby pink "over-blush" spreading across the cheeks and bridge of the nose.
Nose & Lips: Small slim nose with soft contour; "cherry pink" glossy jelly lips with a gradient (darker on the inside); well-defined cupid's bow.
Expression: Innocent, cute, and youthful.
Hair:
Length & Color: Very long, dark brown hair.
Texture: Smooth and shiny.
Style: Straight on top, wavy/curly at the bottom.
Bangs: curtain bangs,dan helaian rambut menutupi wajahnya,slightly messy on top.
Bagian atasnya sedikit berantakan
Environment & Quality:
Background: Dark indoor setting, showing a blurred door and sofa.
Atmosphere: Nighttime.
Lighting: Direct flash focusing on the subject, especially the face, creating a bright and glowing effect.
Technical Quality: HD, 8k high resolution.
Aspect Ratio: 9:16.
Don't change face
```

    }
  },

### 59. Z 世代反审美餐厅自拍

**作者**: [Human AI Gallery | Prompt Architect](https://x.com/HumanAIGallery/status/2028149284256743730)  **日期**: 2026-03-01  **语言**: en

> ```json
> {
>   "prompt": "在深夜快餐店拍摄的垂直、0.5 倍超广角抓拍闪光自拍。主体是一位 20 岁女孩，具有“怪女孩”审美，照片采用刺眼的光线、桶形畸变，以及混乱、未经修饰的细节，以模仿 Z 世代的照片堆风格。",
>   "style": [
>     "垂直构图",
>     "0.5 倍超广角",
>     "抓拍",
>     "闪光自拍",
>     "深夜快餐店背景",
>     "主体：20 岁女孩",
>     "审美：'怪女孩' (weird-girl aesthetic)",
>     "光线：刺眼 (harsh lighting)",
>     "效果：桶形畸变 (barrel distortion)",
>     "细节：混乱、未经修饰 (chaotic, unretouched details)",
>     "风格：模仿 Z 世代照片堆 (Gen-Z photo dump style)"
>   ]
> }
> ```

![Z 世代反审美餐厅自拍](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1772433517475_f4c8te_HCVvBrAWUAAKTZ3.jpg)

```
{
  "image_prompt": {
    "meta": {
      "aspect_ratio": "9:16",
      "style": "0.5x ultra-wide candid flash, late-night fast food"
    },
    "subject": {
      "description": "20-year-old girl with an effortless 'weird-girl' aesthetic",
      "face": "Looking directly into the flash with a bored, deadpan expression, biting the tip of a french fry, messy lip gloss",
      "skin": "Overexposed by the harsh flash, shiny cheeks, authentic and unretouched",
      "hair": "Messy hair tucked under a colorful knitted beanie, large wired headphones worn over the beanie",
      "pose": "Slumped in a bright red plastic diner booth, holding the phone high for a 0.5x selfie, the french fry looking massive in the foreground due to distortion",
      "outfit": "Oversized vintage zip-up hoodie, lots of enamel pins, layered silver rings"
    },
    "environment": {
      "location": "A retro-style 24/7 fast-food joint at 3 AM",
      "background_elements": [
        "A red plastic tray filled with messy burger wrappers and spilled ketchup",
        "Bright, sterile fluorescent lights and a neon window sign in the blur",
        "Checkered linoleum floor reflecting the flash"
      ]
    },
    "lighting": {

**作者**: [Danna R.](https://x.com/daaaaanc/status/2027210994297290836)  **日期**: 2026-02-27  **语言**: en

> 一个针对 Gemini Nano Banana 2 的高度详细提示，侧重于生成具有特定技术参数（iPhone 17 Pro、35mm、f/2.8）和美学增强（用于皮肤/下颌线的“焕颜协议”Glow-Up Protocol）的自然照片。它描述了一位身着科技感黑白分层服装的女性，坐在一间像素完美的室内环境中。

![适用于 Gemini Nano Banana 2 的自然照片生成提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1772259936694_ed6xvk_HCIZpaQaQAEfTIM.jpg)

```
(9:16). Raw iPhone 17 Pro, 35mm, f/2.8, natural bokeh, digital grain. Identity Lock Image A + Glow-Up Protocol: zero-imperfection porcelain skin, zero acne/ojeras, 20% slimmed architectural jawline and cheekbone definition. Salon-finish straight brunette hair. Outfit: Technical black V-neck rib-knit top with high-tensile fit; layered with a cream-colored architectural open-weave crochet cardigan featuring intricate lace patterns. Accessories: Realistic 3D high-fidelity fish pendant on a black technical cord; red star-shaped brooch with white dot details and gold metallic framing on the left chest. Hyper-defined silhouette, 20% anatomical bust volume and waist-to-bust ratio emphasis. Pose: Seated frontal torso alignment, relaxed shoulders. Lighting: Soft indoor 3000K ambient light, ray-traced shadow physics from pendant and cardigan weave. Environment: Pixel-perfect indoor setting: teal-green wall panels with white molding, beige upholstered seating, black technical bag (lower right), light wood table surface (bottom margin).
```

### 79. 三联画式转型之旅艺术作品提示

**作者**: [Cherry 2.O](https://x.com/Mind_Boticni/status/2024080204965224847)  **日期**: 2026-02-18  **语言**: en

> 一个多部分提示，旨在生成一个三格画作，描绘一位年轻女性的象征性蜕变之旅，详细说明了每个画格的背景、姿势和情感基调：“静止 / 起源”、“当下 / 成长”和“自由 / 表达”。

![三联画式转型之旅艺术作品提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1771483134444_koi4ui_HBb6NVHbgAArSmD.jpg)
![三联画式转型之旅艺术作品提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1771483134468_fhntyy_HBb6ILnboAEV3EW.jpg)

```
Create a three-panel grid artwork showing a beautiful young woman portrayed as a symbolic journey of transformation. Each panel must feature a different pose, setting, and emotional tone while clearly showing it is the same person.
Left Panel — “Stillness / Origins”

A beautiful woman with short dark hair, luminous skin, and striking eyes sits on a large stone beside a calm lake at sunrise.

She is shown in a relaxed seated pose, slightly turned away from the viewer, looking toward the horizon.

She wears a soft flowing pastel dress with elegant folds.

The background features misty water, distant hills, and warm early sunlight.

The mood should feel quiet, reflective, and poetic — symbolizing beginnings and inner calm.
Center Panel — “Presence / Becoming”

The same woman now stands confidently in a modern city rooftop garden at golden hour.

She faces forward with a powerful but natural stance, one hand lightly touching her hair as it moves in the wind.

Her outfit becomes more refined: a stylish flowing dress with subtle contemporary elegance.

Background includes skyline silhouettes, soft sunlight, and greenery, symbolizing growth, awareness, and stepping into life.
Right Panel — “Freedom / Expression”

The same woman is shown in motion on a dramatic coastal cliff with the ocean behind her.

She is captured mid-spin or mid-stride, hair and dress flowing strongly in the wind.

Her pose should feel energetic, open, and fearless.

Background shows crashing waves, wide sky, and dynamic light — symbolizing liberation, expansion, and self-realization.
```

**Related**: [[综合艺术]]、[[城市场景]]、[[奇幻世界]]

### 82. 奥本海默场景换脸与修复

**作者**: [Mahesh](https://x.com/Mahesh171819/status/2023649817227141359)  **日期**: 2026-02-17  **语言**: en

> 一个高度具体的提示，指示 AI 重现电影《奥本海默》中的一个精确帧（构图、灯光、表情、服装和姿态），并仅将基里安·墨菲的脸替换为上传的参考脸，要求达到超现实的电影级真实感，且不允许任何创作自由。

![奥本海默场景换脸与修复](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1771396574358_u3mlnt_HBVyyFJbcAEeA4Q.jpg)
![奥本海默场景换脸与修复](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1771396574353_unptgc_HBVyx8YbcAQpnAT.jpg)

```
Use the uploaded Oppenheimer movie frame as the PRIMARY and ONLY scene reference.

Reproduce the scene EXACTLY as shown:
same interior room and background blur,
same soft daylight from camera-left,
same muted green–yellow color temperature,
same camera angle and proximity (tight close-up),
same framing and crop,
same shallow depth of field,
same outfit (teal shirt, dark tie),
same hand-to-temple gesture,
same ring on finger,
same anxious, mentally strained expression,
same eye direction and tension,
same posture and head tilt.

DO NOT reinterpret the scene.
DO NOT change the environment, lighting, or composition.

Replace ONLY the face with my uploaded face reference.
My face must remain 100% identical:
exact facial structure,
skin tone,
eye shape,
nose,
lips,
jawline,
hairline,
stubble pattern preserved.

Face swap must perfectly match:
original head angle,
original facial muscle tension,
original eye direction,
original lighting and shadow falloff.

Ultra-realistic cinematic realism.
Natural film grain preserved.
No stylization, no creative liberty.

Aspect ratio: 1.90:1 (IMAX digital frame).
Full headroom preserved.
No crop, no zoom, no reframing.
No background change
No lighting change
No pose change
No hand movement
No expression change
No color grading
No stylization
No AI artifacts
No face morphing
No resemblance to Cillian Murphy
```

### 86. 电影胶片剧照网格提示，用于家庭舞蹈场景

**作者**: [Özge Döner](https://x.com/astronomerozge1/status/2023086953428607098)  **日期**: 2026-02-15  **语言**: en

> 一个详细的 JSON 提示，用于 Nano Banana Pro 生成一个 2x3 网格的电影胶片剧照，捕捉亲密的家庭舞蹈场景。该提示指定了复杂的参数，包括图生图模式、身份和姿势的保留、特定照明（温暖柔和的环境光）、相机设置（35mm, f/2.0）以及详细的主体服装（深红色缎面连衣裙）和运动模糊控制。

![电影胶片剧照网格提示，用于家庭舞蹈场景](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1771223960099_57p2kr_HBNy2wGWwAEVfw7.jpg)

```
{
  "generation_request": {
    "meta_data": {
      "task_type": "home_dance_film_still_grid_2x3_red_satin",
      "language": "en",
      "priority": "highest",
      "version": "v1.0_HOME_DANCE_2X3_RED_SATIN_FILM"
    },
    "input": {
      "mode": "image_to_image",
      "reference_image_usage": "very_high",
      "preserve_identity": true,
      "preserve_facial_features": true,
      "preserve_pose_dynamics": true,
      "notes": "Use the reference collage as the primary anchor. Keep the same couple, same room, same framing and dance flow across six panels. Change the woman's dress to a deep red satin dress with elegant sheen. Maintain realistic motion blur from dancing while keeping faces readable."
    },
    "output": {
      "aspect_ratio": "1:1",
      "resolution": "ultra_high",
      "num_images": 1,
      "layout": {
        "type": "grid",
        "rows": 2,
        "cols": 3,
        "gutter": "thin",
        "panel_consistency": "high"
      },
      "sharpness": "filmic_soft",
      "grain": "subtle_analog",
      "halation": "soft"
    },
    "scene": {
      "concept": "intimate home dance sequence captured as cinematic film stills",
      "environment": "cozy interior hallway/living room, simple door and framed picture on wall, warm daylight or tungsten mix",
      "lighting": {
        "style": "warm soft ambient light",
        "key_light": "window-like soft side light",
        "fill_light": "gentle fill to keep skin detail",
        "shadow_behavior": "soft, slightly hazy",
        "avoid": "hard flash, harsh HDR"
      },
      "camera": {
        "lens": "35mm",
        "aperture": "f/2.0",
        "depth_of_field": "shallow to medium",
        "look": "vintage film still, slight softness and bloom"
      }
    },
    "subjects": {
      "count": 2,
      "type": "adult couple",
      "male": {
        "wardrobe": "white fitted t-shirt, dark trousers",

### 95. 卧室里的颗粒感 iPhone 自拍

**作者**: [babydoll](https://x.com/bananababydoll/status/2020961652758515772)  **日期**: 2026-02-09  **语言**: en

![卧室里的颗粒感 iPhone 自拍](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1770706213050_9vsca7_G_q7izgXwAEXpl4.jpg)

```
{
  "meta": {
    "quality": "ultra photorealistic",
    "resolution": "8k",
    "camera": "iPhone 15 Pro",
    "lens": "26mm",
    "aspect_ratio": "4:3",
    "style": "warm lamp, grainy iphone look"
  },

  "character_lock": {
    "age": "mid 20s",
    "ethnicity": "blonde european",
    "hair": { "color": "blonde", "style": "messy ponytail" },
    "eyes": "blue",
    "body": { "type": "curvy", "chest": "heavy", "waist": "tiny", "hips": "round" }
  },

  "scene": {
    "location": "bedroom floor",
    "time": "late night"
  },

  "subject": {
    "action": "sitting on floor taking selfie",
    "pose": {
      "knees_bent": true,
      "one_hand": "lifting shirt",
      "expression": "biting lower lip"
    },

    "outfit": {
      "top": {
        "type": "oversized t-shirt",
        "color": "{argument name="t-shirt color" default="white"}",
        "fit": "braless"
      },
      "bottom": {
        "type": "cotton thong",
        "color": "{argument name="thong color" default="pink"}"
      }

### 96. 书店过道里的胶片之吻

**作者**: [Özge Döner](https://x.com/astronomerozge1/status/2020621120274125095)  **日期**: 2026-02-08  **语言**: en

> 一个高度具体的 JSON 提示，用于生成一张亲密、坦诚的模拟胶片照片，内容是一对情侣在傍晚时分，在狭窄的书店过道里接吻。它详细描述了拍摄对象的服装、姿势、灯光（暖钨丝灯，昏暗舒适的氛围）和相机设置（35mm 复古定焦镜头，柯达 Portra 400 增感 +1），以实现一种情绪化、高质感、真实的胶片效果，包括对逼真解剖结构的限制。

![书店过道里的胶片之吻](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1770619745414_y86vhw_HAqwMWVbkAAoEBX.jpg)

```
{
  "meta": {
    "project": "analog_library_kiss",
    "style": "analog_film_intimate_candid",
    "aspect_ratio": "{argument name="aspect ratio" default="3:4"}",
    "output_type": "single_image",
    "priority": "highest"
  },
  "scene": {
    "location": "narrow used-book bookstore / small library aisle",
    "time": "evening",
    "lighting": "warm tungsten practicals, dim cozy ambience, soft falloff into shadows",
    "composition": "shot through a foreground gap between stacked books (foreground heavily blurred), couple centered mid-frame, bookshelves filling the background, claustrophobic intimate framing"
  },
  "subjects": {
    "male": {
      "age": "mid 20s",
      "outfit": "light beige button-up shirt with sleeves down, casual",
      "pose": "left arm around her waist pulling her close, head tilted toward her",
      "expression": "eyes closed, kissing"
    },
    "female": {
      "age": "mid 20s",
      "outfit": "light beige/taupe sleeveless dress",
      "hair": "long dark wavy hair, loose, slightly messy",
      "pose": "both arms up around his neck, fingers in his hair/neckline, leaning in",
      "expression": "eyes closed, kissing"
    }
  },
  "motion_language": {
    "feel": "candid handheld moment",
    "blur": "intentional slight motion blur on faces/arms from movement during the kiss, not smeared or warped"
  },
  "camera": {
    "lens": "35mm vintage prime",
    "distance": "close-medium",
    "angle": "eye-level, slightly off-center",
    "focus": "focus on their heads/upper bodies, shallow depth of field; foreground books very soft bokeh",
    "exposure": "low light, natural grain, highlights protected (no blown lamps)"
  },
  "analog_look": {
    "film_stock": "{argument name="film stock" default="Kodak Portra 400 pushed +1 moody"}",
    "grain": "visible organic grain, film-like",
    "contrast": "low-mid, lifted blacks",
    "color": "warm amber highlights, muted greens/browns in shadows",
    "halation": "subtle around specular highlights on book edges",
    "softness": "gentle lens softness + slight corner falloff, not digital blur",
    "imperfections": "very light vignette, tiny dust specks, mild gate weave feel"
  },
  "texture_fidelity": {
    "skin": "natural pores and sheen, no plastic smoothing",
    "fabric": "visible weave and folds, realistic shadowing",
    "books": "paper edges, worn spines, readable texture but no readable text emphasis"
  },
  "constraints": {
    "perfect_anatomy": true,
    "correct_fingers": true,
    "no_extra_limbs": true,
    "no_face_morphing": true,
    "no_face_swapping": true,
    "no_weird_teeth": true,
    "no_background_warp": true,
    "no_text_overlay": true,
    "no_logos": true,
    "no_cgi_look": true,
    "no_beauty_filter": true
  },
  "negative": "HDR, over-sharpened, glossy skin, AI-symmetry face, duplicated faces, melted hands, extra fingers, warped shelves, floating books, neon colors, strong vignette, heavy light leaks, digital bokeh circles, poster text, watermark"
}
```

### 103. 参考图像的服装替换工作流程

**作者**: [Shine by Nous ✨](https://x.com/Shinebynous/status/2018762285171319105)  **日期**: 2026-02-03  **语言**: en

> 描述了使用 Gemini 3 和 Nano Banana Pro 来保持角色身份，同时迭代更换服装的工作流程。初始提示会根据参考图像更改服装，后续迭代则使用新生成的图像作为基础进行进一步的服装更改。

![参考图像的服装替换工作流程](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1770187185646_9rs5s7_HAQHhNCXYAAovQK.jpg)

```
I started with two reference images and a simple first prompt:
" Change the clothes of the woman to the {argument name="new outfit" default="yellow and green outfit"}, keep her face the same" 

Once I had that result, I reused the generated image as the new base. 
I added a fresh outfit reference and kept the prompt structure identical, only changing the outfit name:

"Change outfit to [NAME] outfit"
```

> 一个用于生成高级个人品牌英雄图像的提示，采用无缝双联画风格，主角为 ROSÉ (BLACKPINK) 和 Bruno Mars。它指定了 16:9 的宽高比、连续的渐变背景（勃艮第色到象牙色）、编辑级美学，并详细描述了他们的服装、发型、妆容、姿势（彼此相对），以及包含微妙的文本叠加。

![ROSÉ 和 Bruno Mars 双联画英雄图片](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1770100830447_caskxi_HAJ25xjagAAF8z_.jpg)
![ROSÉ 和 Bruno Mars 双联画英雄图片](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1770100830815_qh9nn9_HAJ2poJbAAA9CWT.jpg)

```
Premium personal branding hero image in diptych style with 16:9 aspect ratio. Single seamless canvas with two poses side by side, no frames, no borders, no panels. Single continuous gradient background flowing from {argument name="left color" default="deep burgundy"} on the left to {argument name="right color" default="soft cream ivory"} on the right, no separation, no frames, full-bleed. Soft diffused light consistent across entire canvas. Editorial beauty campaign aesthetic, seamless tone-on-tone. Magazine cover quality. Intimate mood with mirrored symmetry.
The subjects are {argument name="subject 1" default="ROSÉ, BLACKPINK member"}, and {argument name="subject 2" default="Bruno Mars, singer"}. Both have oval face, high cheekbones, flawless porcelain skin with glass-skin finish. ROSÉ has blonde soft waves framing face, Bruno Mars has curly black hair. Minimal dewy makeup with nude pink glossy lips. ROSÉ wears cream ivory chunky knit sweater, Bruno Mars wears deep burgundy velvet blazer, black shirt, and black fedora hat.
ROSÉ and Bruno Mars face toward the center, looking at each other. ROSÉ is touching her cheek with her hand, with "ROSÉ" text in elegant serif typeface similar to Didot or Times New Roman, light weight, small size, at bottom left. Bruno Mars is holding his fedora hat with his hand, with "Bruno Mars" text in elegant serif typeface similar to Didot or Times New Roman, light weight, small size, at bottom right.

### 105. 沙滩躺椅后视扭转姿势

**作者**: [brindley](https://x.com/brindleyai/status/2017993931842081279)  **日期**: 2026-02-01  **语言**: en

> 一个详细的 JSON 提示，用于生成一张高质量的海滨度假村生活方式照片。照片描绘了一位年轻女性，身穿白色细带比基尼，坐在躺椅上，身体背对镜头，扭头回望。提示强调了刺眼的阳光，以突显肌肉线条和臀部丰满度。

```
{
"subject": {
"description": "Young woman with a fit, tanned, and curvy physique, viewed from the back while seated.",
"hair": "Long blonde hair with highlights, darker roots, worn down and slightly tousled by the wind, sunglasses perched on top of the head.",
"outfit": "White textured crinkle-fabric string bikini. The bottoms are thong-style with a high cut, exposing the glutes. The top features thin white string ties visible across the back and tied at the neck.",
"body_details": "Prominent and full gluteal volume, athletic back definition, slim waist, visible spine indentation. Skin texture shows natural tan lines and smooth surface with realistic light reflection.",
"facial_features": "Profile visible as she turns her head over her left shoulder, bright white smile, defined jawline, wearing small hoop earrings."
},
"pose": {
"type": "Seated rear-view twist.",
"details": "Subject is sitting on a beach lounger covered with a white towel. Her body is angled away from the camera (rear view). She twists her torso to the left to look back over her left shoulder towards the viewer. Her right arm extends downwards, hand resting on the edge of the lounger. Legs are bent beneath her.",
"alignment": "Spine is arched, shoulders are pulled back, head is tilted slightly upward and to the left."
},
"environment": {
"location": "Sunny sandy beach resort.",

### 107. Q 版角色操作赛博窗口提示

**作者**: [Yukinobu Kurata : 倉田幸暢](https://x.com/YukinobuKurata/status/2017465645504577882)  **日期**: 2026-01-31  **语言**: ja

> 一个高度详细、结构化的 Nano Banana Pro 提示词，用于生成一个在赛博空间中操作半透明窗口的动漫风格 Q 版女孩。该提示词包含关于角色表情、头发、AR 眼镜、服装、姿势、周围物体、背景和艺术风格的具体细节，包括文本叠加。

![Q 版角色操作赛博窗口提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1769927696289_pctb8t_G_95gZAbEAEDZPk.jpg)
![Q 版角色操作赛博窗口提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1769927696615_s971mp_GzUEOWEa4AQTvLf.jpg)

```
## 全体のコンセプト
concept: "サイバー空間で浮遊する半透明のウィンドウ（ディスプレイ）を操作することに夢中になっている、笑顔がかわいいちびキャラの女の子"

## 主体となるキャラクターの詳細
subject:
  type: "ちびキャラのアニメスタイルの女の子"
  reference: "添付画像のキャラクターデザインのレファレンスシートにもとづいたキャラクターデザインにする"
  expression: "目を輝かせ、発見や楽しさに満ちた満面の笑顔"
  hair:
    details: "髪の一部がデータ粒子のように淡く発光している"
  wearables:
    - item: "ARグラス"
      type: "フレームレスなバイザースタイル"
      material: "非常に透明度が高く、クリスタルのような質感の半透明素材"
      details: "グラスの縁が細いネオンブルーのラインで発光しており、彼女の視界に情報を投影している"
  outfit:
    style: "袖口の内側には電子回路のような幾何学模様がサイアン色でプリントされている"
  direction: "画像の左側を向いている"

## キャラクターのアクションとポーズ
action:
  verb: "ウィンドウ（ディスプレイ）を操作する"
  pose: "サイバー空間にふわりと座るように浮遊し、少し前のめりの姿勢で、空中に浮かんでいる半透明のウィンドウ（ディスプレイ）を操作している"
  hands: "指先を軽やかに動かし、空中に浮かんでいる半透明のウィンドウ（ディスプレイ）を操作している"

## 周辺オブジェクト
objects:
  - item: "空中に浮かんでいる複数の半透明のウィンドウ"
    type: "半透明のインターフェース"
    shape: "緩やかなカーブを描くワイドスクリーン"
    content: "そのウィンドウのなかに、カラフルな一覧リスト」が、透けて見えている。"
    details: "ウィンドウ（ディスプレイ）は半透明なため、その後ろにあるキャラクターの姿や背景が透けて見える"

## 背景と環境
environment:
  setting: "抽象的でミニマルなサイバースペース"
  background:
    color: "黒色"
    details:
      - "キャラクターの背景に、キャラクターを中心とした、白色のベタフラッシュ（ひとつひとつのトゲがとても細く尖っている）が描かれている。"
      - "彼女の周囲を、小さなデータの光の粒子や、半透明の立方体がゆっくりと漂っている"
    text:
      - "画面右上：縦書きで、「やはり Sticky ToC・・・・」の大きな文字。（「Sticky ToC」の文字は、横書きで表示する。）"
      - "画面左上：縦書きで、「Sticky ToC は \n 全てを解決する・・・・！！」の大きな文字。（「Sticky ToC」の文字は、横書きで表示する。）"

## アートスタイルと品質
style:
  art_style: "高品質なアニメイラストレーション、滑らかな線画と鮮やかな色彩"
  lighting: "キャラクター自身と彼女が操作するウィンドウ（ディスプレイ）が主要な光源。顔や体にディスプレイからの柔らかい反射光が当たっている。全体的に明るく、クリーンな印象。"
  color_palette: "白をベースに、パステルピンク、エメラルドグリーン、サイバーな青とシアンをアクセントカラーとして使用"
  effects: "グロー（発光）効果、ブルーム効果を適度に加える"
  quality: "最高品質, 傑作, 超高解像度, 精細なディテール"
```

Physical Features: The character has a very fit voluptuos hourglass physique and smooth skin. 

Outfit and Accessory Details

### 112. 天元突破风格的“Gaina-Dachi”动漫姿势提示

**作者**: [SSSS_CRYPTOMAN](https://x.com/SSSS_CRYPTOMAN/status/2016798514639212928)  **日期**: 2026-01-29  **语言**: en

> 一个详细的提示，旨在生成一张具有《天元突破 红莲螺岩》风格（Gaina-Dachi 姿势）的爆炸性、高冲击力动漫插画。它着重于强烈的情感、动态的向上风效、大胆的线条，并包含一个特定的手写日文毛笔字叠加。

![天元突破风格的“Gaina-Dachi”动漫姿势提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1769755042792_wwwl13_G_0bjuObUAAWdlp.jpg)

```
Consistent character from reference image: exact same face, hairstyle, body shape, and original outfit. NO redesign.

[Composition & Pose]:
Heroic and exaggerated anime stance, waist-up framing, front-facing. Arms tightly crossed, chest pushed forward, leaning slightly towards the camera to create intense pressure. High visual density.

[Expression]:
Explosive emotion, intense anger mixed with determination. Mouth wide open shouting, eyebrows sharply angled, piercing eyes with sharp highlights.

[Dynamic Motion]:
A violent upward wind blasting from below the character,
powerful vertical airflow pushing both fabric and hair upward and outward.
The original clothing from the reference image remains intact and reacts naturally to the force,
all loose parts of the outfit whipping and flaring aggressively,
the character’s hair is lifted, blown upward, and spread by the same updraft,
hair strands follow the vertical flow with dynamic, forceful motion,
movement extends beyond the frame,
the motion feels heavy, chaotic, and explosive,
as if the character is standing in a violent upward draft.

[Art Style]:
Bold anime illustration, thick and rough energetic linework, expressive hand-drawn strokes. High contrast, dramatic cel-shading. Focus on raw emotion and impact.

[Background & Text]:
Solid white background.
Behind the character, ONE single instance of large handwritten Japanese brush text.
The text must appear ONCE only, not repeated, not duplicated.
All characters must be fully visible, complete, and readable.
No missing strokes, no cropped characters, no broken parts.

The text is continuous and written as one complete phrase:
「{argument name="セリフ" default="俺を誰だと思っていやがる！"}」

Pure hand-painted brush lettering, NOT a font.
Wild, uneven brush strokes with controlled ink splatter and wobble,
but the structure of each character remains intact. Black ink only.

[Technical]:
High-impact poster visual, anime key visual style, ultra-high resolution, 8k.
```

**Related**: [[手绘素描]]、[[综合艺术]]、[[综合设计]]

### 113. 悉尼·斯威尼 (Sydney Sweeney) 双重时尚造型提示

**作者**: [Bahar azam](https://x.com/BaharAzamm561/status/2016741958073667866)  **日期**: 2026-01-29  **语言**: en

> 一个结构化的 JSON 提示，旨在生成两张悉尼·斯威尼 (Sydney Sweeney) 的不同时尚图片：一张是她在都市夜景中身着单色牛仔套装，搭配结构化细节的造型；另一张是她在正式红毯活动中，身着高级定制礼服，头戴薄纱蝴蝶结发带的造型。

### 114. 极简流程图/图表生成风格指南

**作者**: [Zephyr.在思考丨阿杭杭杭](https://x.com/Astronaut_1216/status/2016498493909524833)  **日期**: 2026-01-28  **语言**: zh

> 一份详细的 Nano Banana Pro 风格指南提示，用于生成极简、清晰的流程图或图表。它规定了调色板、线条类型（正交）、形状（圆角矩形、菱形）和排版，以确保专业、一致且易于阅读的信息图风格。

![极简流程图/图表生成风格指南](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1769668517280_07mg8l_G_uvxYjWkAEtjek.jpg)

```
生成图片，1. 风格核心参数提取 (Style Guide)
请参照以下参数：
配色 (Color Palette):
背景: 纯白 (#FFFFFF)
线条/边框: 深灰或纯黑 (#333333 或 #000000)
文字: 深灰 (#333333)，字重常规，无加粗。
填充: 无填充（透明）或纯白填充，以遮挡背后的线条。
线条 (Lines/Connectors):
类型: 正交线 (Orthogonal/Elbow)，即只有垂直和水平线，拐角为直角。
粗细: 极细 (1px)。
箭头: 实心小三角 (Solid Arrowhead)，黑色。
形状 (Shapes):
普通节点: 圆角矩形 (Rounded Rectangle)，圆角半径很小 (约 4px - 8px)。
判断节点: 菱形 (Diamond)。
开始/结束: 胶囊形或圆角更大的矩形。
排版 (Typography):
对齐: 居中对齐。
字体: 无衬线字体 (Sans-serif)，如 Arial, Roboto 或思源黑体。字号较小 (约 12px-14px)。

上面的风格加上你的用户旅程/流程给到gemini，那么他就会呈现相应的效果给你，调都不用调
```

**Related**: [[数据可视化]]、[[综合图表]]、[[综合设计]]

> 一个详细的 JSON 提示，用于使用 Gemini Nano Banana Pro 模型生成一张逼真的、高分辨率的女性（Sydney Sweeney）在泳池环境中的图像。该提示细致地定义了拍摄对象的样貌、姿势（倚靠在泳池甲板上）和服装——一件高光泽、双色调的皇家粉和泡泡糖蓝竞技泳衣。它还指定了热带度假村环境、明亮的高调自然光照和强烈的镜面高光，以及 3:4 宽高比的中景全身镜头。

The material has a high-shine, latex-like or wet lycra finish. A small pink logo is visible on the upper chest."

Further back, there is a poolside patio with white lounge chairs, lush green hedges, palm trees, and a villa-style structure with a wooden pergola roof, evoking a tropical summer atmosphere."
  },
  "lighting_and_shot": {

The image is sharp and high-resolution with a shallow depth of field that keeps the subject in crisp focus while slightly blurring the background elements. Aspect Ratio {argument name="aspect ratio" default="3:4"}."
  }
}

### 119. Nano Banana Pro 手写生成提示词

**作者**: [そーじろー｜デザイン兄さん](https://x.com/SojiroNishi/status/2016254385118969890)  **日期**: 2026-01-27  **语言**: en

> 这是一个为 Nano Banana Pro 设计的详细提示，旨在生成一行具有特定女性化、时尚和飘逸美感的日文手写文本。它指定了书写工具（细凝胶笔）、笔画特征（纤细、轻盈、单线），并引入了字符大小、间距和基线倾斜的有意不规则性，以模仿自然手写。该提示明确要求提供参考图像以指导风格，并包含一个负面提示，以避免毛笔/书法风格。

![Nano Banana Pro 手写生成提示词](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1769582030644_le72bb_G_o0py4akAABSoj.jpg)
![Nano Banana Pro 手写生成提示词](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1769582030656_wvjglo_G_o0mDZWIAA2HvF.jpg)
![Nano Banana Pro 手写生成提示词](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1769582030705_89hdgg_G_o0ohSbwAAWEAS.jpg)
![Nano Banana Pro 手写生成提示词](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1769582031246_vbt6rr_G_o0rPjbgAA-mzz.jpg)

```
Use the attached reference images as the handwriting style guide (especially the second image with handwriting samples). Create a single line of Japanese handwritten text on clean white paper. Written with a fine gel pen / fineliner (0.3–0.4mm look), thin and light strokes, mostly monoline (no brush or marker look). Match a stylish, airy, feminine handwriting feel: soft curves, light touch, and a slightly right-leaning slant.Add clear personality through noticeable character size variation (some characters 10–25% larger/smaller), irregular spacing, and a gentle upward baseline from left to right. Add elongated entry and exit strokes (long, tapered starts/tails) on a few characters—especially the first character, any elongated/extended marks in the text, and the final character—while keeping everything readable.Write exactly this text: 「{argument name="text to write" default="本命チョコはオトナの味がした。"}」No extra text, no borders, no logos, no underline, no decorative swoosh lines. High resolution, sharp thin ink lines, minimal paper texture.
Negative：
brush pen, calligraphy, shodo, marker, thick strokes, bold ink, heavy pressure, paintbrush, blocky lettering, uniform character size, perfect spacing, perfectly straight baseline, printed font, typeset, outline font, extra words, watermark, frame, stamps, underline, swoosh line, doodles
Extra：
Keep strokes thin; create expressiveness mainly with size/spacing/baseline and tapered stroke ends, not thickness.Increase character size contrast and spacing irregularity, but keep legibility.
```

**Related**: [[浮世绘与日本传统]]、[[手绘素描]]、[[综合艺术]]

### 121. 西德尼·斯威尼 (Sydney Sweeney) 在奢华内饰中的超焦距原片

### 125. Barbiecore 巴黎·希尔顿 街头风格 (JSON 格式)

**作者**: [bengi](https://x.com/p3rikly/status/2015547470269309051)  **日期**: 2026-01-25  **语言**: en

> 一个详细的 JSON 提示，用于生成一张高饱和度、具有“芭比风”的图像，内容是 {argument name="celebrity" default="Paris Hilton"} 身穿粉色两件套服装，置身于阳光普照的比弗利山庄街道上。该提示指定了高角度拍摄、9:16 的垂直长宽比，以及将主体缩短并使背景扁平化的技术指令，以强调强烈阳光和锐利阴影。

![Barbiecore 巴黎·希尔顿 街头风格 (JSON 格式)](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1769408688397_023xxr_G_ipusjXEAA2K9p.jpg)

```
{
  "image_generation_parameters": {
    "subject": {
      "description": "{argument name="celebrity" default="Paris Hilton"} with long wavy hair",
      "attire": "Pink two-piece outfit consisting of a bustier crop top and a pleated mini skirt",
      "accessories": ["White retro cat-eye sunglasses", "Small pink woven handbag"],
      "pose": "Standing beside a car, smiling upward, one hand near her face and the other holding a bag"
    },
    "environment": {
      "setting": "Sun-drenched Beverly Hills style street",
      "background_elements": ["Tall palm trees lining a residential road", "Clear blue sky", "Green hedges"],
      "prop": "Pink vintage convertible car with detailed interior and chrome steering wheel"
    },
    "cinematography": {
      "camera_angle": "High-angle shot (looking down from above)",
      "framing": "Medium Close-Up (MCU) focusing on head, torso, and top of the car",
      "aspect_ratio": "9:16 (Vertical)",
      "lens_effect": "Standard 50mm focal length to minimize distortion while emphasizing height"
    },
    "lighting_and_color": {
      "aesthetic": "Vibrant, high-saturation, 'Barbiecore' aesthetic",
      "lighting": "Hard, direct sunlight creating sharp shadows on the asphalt road",
      "primary_palette": ["Bubblegum Pink", "Bright White", "Asphalt Gray", "Palm Green"]
    },
    "technical_directive": "Re-render the original scene with a dramatic perspective shift. Foreshorten the subject's body to show visual dominance from the high-angle position. Ensure the car's pink dashboard and the road surface appear flattened beneath the subject."
  }
}
```

> 一个高度结构化的 JSON 提示词，用于 Gemini Nano Banana Pro 生成一张超写实编辑图片，描绘两名女性（萨迪·辛克/米莉·芭比·布朗 和 亚历山德拉·达达里奥/杜阿·利帕 风格）穿着配套的紧身胸衣式迷你连衣裙，在豪华步入式衣帽间内摆姿势，采用直射闪光摄影和高对比度。

> 一个用于 Nano Banana Pro（通过 Hailuo AI）的 JSON 提示，旨在创作一张电影风格的拼贴画，内容是三张身穿闪亮红色迷你连衣裙的迷人年轻女性（安娜·德·阿玛斯风格）的照片，捕捉 2000 年代派对氛围，带有闪光摄影和复古胶片质感。

  "subject": {
    "description": "Glamorous young girl",
    "hair": "Long hair",
    "hair_note": "Do not change original hair color",
    "vibe": "It-girl"
  },

      "id": 1,
      "shot_type": "Dark silhouette",

### 131. 逼真的照片与体素《我的世界》分身

**作者**: [Mohamed IDBRAHIM](https://x.com/brightcoding/status/2014836135130788042)  **日期**: 2026-01-23  **语言**: en

> 这是一个图像生成提示，旨在创建一张高度逼真的照片：一个人站在白雪皑皑的山景中，穿着厚实的羽绒服。独特的元素是，一个真人大小的 3D Minecraft 风格体素角色站在他们旁边，其穿着与真实人物的服装完美匹配。该提示强调电影级光照、8K 画质，以及照片级真实感与简洁体素艺术风格之间的对比。它明确要求提供参考图像以保留人物身份。

![逼真的照片与体素《我的世界》分身](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1769236046609_yambru_G_YixvHWEAEGdC1.jpg)

```
Use the attached reference image to create a realistic photo of the same person, with identity perfectly preserved and no facial changes.
The person is standing in a snowy mountain landscape, without sunglasses, wearing a thick puffer jacket in a {argument name="jacket color" default="random color"}.
Beside him stands a life-size 3D Minecraft-style character version of the same person, made entirely of blocks (voxel style), wearing the exact same puffer jacket in the same {argument name="jacket color 2" default="random color"}, perfectly matching the real outfit.
The lighting is cinematic and natural, with realistic shadows and highlights.
High resolution, 8K quality.
Photorealistic style for the real person, contrasted with clean voxel art for the Minecraft character.
Sharp focus, professional color grading.
```

> 一个详细的提示，用于生成一个皮克斯/迪士尼风格的 3D 风格化角色，重点突出柔和的特征、富有表现力的眼睛、舒适时尚的现代服装，以及 Octane/Arnold 风格和 8K 分辨率等高质量渲染规格。

![超精细 3D 风格化角色设计提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1769149390493_3akc2w_G_Pq-uHakAEI5re.jpg)

```
Use Reference figuire1 Create Ultra-detailed 3D stylized character design of a cute with a Pixar/Disney-inspired look, soft rounded facial features, big expressive eyes, smooth porcelain skin, and playful proportions.
Outfit is cozy-chic and modern: oversized knitted sweaters, fluffy jackets, cropped tops, skirts or wide-leg jeans, textured fabrics like wool, fleece, and knit, paired with chunky sneakers or plush boots. Warm color palette with pastel and vibrant tones ({argument name="Color Palette" default="orange, teal, purple, yellow"}).
Accessories include a small backpack or sling bag, headphones or goggles, and a cute animal companion (like a {argument name="Animal Companion" default="tiny owl"}) resting on person shoulder. Confident yet relaxed pose, fashion-model stance or playful walking motion.
Rendered in ultra-high-quality 3D, soft studio lighting, smooth gradients, clean solid background colors, shallow depth of field, cinematic composition, highly detailed fabric textures, realistic subsurface scattering, polished toy-like finish, adorable and wholesome aesthetic, premium character art, 8K resolution, Octane/Arnold style render.
```

### 133. 街头抓拍夜景照片提示

**作者**: [babydoll](https://x.com/bananababydoll/status/2014209914072113350)  **日期**: 2026-01-22  **语言**: en

> 一个为 Nano Banana Pro 设计的详细、结构化的提示，旨在生成一张在出租车候客区拍摄的逼真、坦率、深夜街头照片。该提示侧重于实现一种情绪化、略带瑕疵的“真实 iPhone 照片”美学，其中包含关于拍摄对象的外观、姿势、光线和明确的负面约束的具体细节，以确保真实性并避免 AI 伪影。

![街头抓拍夜景照片提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1769149382025_fiec9o_G_NllinXMAA2hpr.jpg)
![街头抓拍夜景照片提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1769149382095_rhvjm5_G_NllihWQAAyvkx.jpg)

```
{
  "meta": {
    "aspect_ratio": "9:16",
    "camera": "iPhone 15 Pro Max",
    "look": "real iPhone photo, candid, slightly imperfect framing"
  },
  "scene": {
    "location": "late-night taxi stand on a wet street (city center)",
    "weather": "light rain, wet asphalt reflections",
    "background": "soft bokeh streetlights, a couple of women blurred far behind, no men",
    "vibe": "messy confidence, a little toxic, don’t-approach energy"
  },
  "lighting": {
    "type": "streetlights + storefront spill + subtle phone flash",
    "feel": "moody but realistic, not cinematic, not studio"
  },
  "camera_perspective": {
    "shot_by": "a female friend",
    "distance": "about 1 meter",
    "angle": "slightly low",
    "framing": "mid-thigh to head, a bit off-center like a real snap",
    "imperfections": "tiny motion blur in background, slight noise in shadows, minor exposure mismatch"
  },
  "subject": {
    "female": true,
    "age": "24 (clearly adult)",
    "ethnicity": "random (non-specific)",
    "beauty_level": "instagram model but real",
    "hair": "dark blonde, loose waves, a bit damp from rain",
    "expression": "side-eye + small smirk, chin slightly up",
    "makeup": "minimal glam, glossy lips, not overdone",
    "pose": "one hip forward, shoulders relaxed, holding phone down by side (screen not visible)",
    "outfit": {
      "top": "thin ribbed long-sleeve top, opaque, braless (no straps, no visible bra lines)",
      "bottom": "low-rise black jeans, realistic folds",
      "shoes": "simple ankle boots"
    }
  },
  "realism": {
    "skin": "natural texture, tiny pores, faint under-eye texture, one small blemish ok",
    "details": "a few flyaway hairs, slight lint on jeans, mild rain specks on sleeves"
  },
  "negative_prompt": [
    "men",
    "nudity",
    "explicit anatomy",
    "pornographic pose",
    "overly perfect plastic skin",
    "super sharp HDR look",
    "text, watermark, logos",
    "extra fingers, deformed hands, face warping"
  ]
}
```

### 134. 2x2 名人照相亭网格提示

**作者**: [Qaiser Tzq](https://x.com/TzqQaiser/status/2014016403930812576)  **日期**: 2026-01-21  **语言**: en

> 一个结构化提示，详细描述了生成一张 2x2 拍立得照片网格，其中包含安娜·德·阿玛斯（Ana de Armas）和西德尼·斯威尼（Sydney Sweeney），并具体说明了她们的服装、发型以及每个象限的四种不同的俏皮互动/姿势（例如，运动姿势、背人、摇滚主题）。

![2x2 名人照相亭网格提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1769063229818_9r1vuj_G_M5OchbkAEOGxo.jpg)

```
{

  "project": "Celebrity_Photo_Booth_Analysis_2026",
  "metadata": {
    "composition_type": "2x2 Image Grid",
    "background_color_hex": "#4A708B",
    "lighting": "Soft Studio Lighting / Flash",
    "subject_count": 2
  },
  "subjects": [
    {
      "id": "subject_01",
      "name": "Ana de Armas",
      "physical_attributes": {
        "hair_color": "Brunette",
        "hair_style": "Wavy, Shoulder-length",
        "outfit": "Black sequined sleeveless mini-dress/top",
        "accessories": "Small silver earrings"
      }
    },
    {
      "id": "subject_02",
      "name": "Sydney Sweeney",
      "physical_attributes": {
        "hair_color": "Blonde",
        "hair_style": "Short bob, wavy",
        "outfit": "Silver/Platinum satin floor-length gown",
        "outfit_detail": "Jeweled/Crystal straps",
        "accessories": "Thin silver necklace"
      }
    }
  ],
  "detailed_grid_breakdown": {
    "quadrant_1_top_left": {
      "interaction": "Athletic Pose",
      "ana_de_armas": {
        "pose": "Bicep flex with both arms",
        "gaze": "Direct to camera",
        "mood": "Playful/Strong"
      },
      "sydney_sweeney": {
        "pose": "Leaning forward, hands out of frame",
        "gaze": "Direct to camera",
        "mood": "Candid/Action"
      }
    },
    "quadrant_2_top_right": {
      "interaction": "Close-up Intimacy",
      "ana_de_armas": {
        "pose": "Bending low, hands on knees",
        "expression": "Sultry/Engaged",
        "focus": "High-angle perspective"
      },
      "sydney_sweeney": {
        "pose": "Head tilted, arm framing the top",
        "expression": "Soft smile",
        "focus": "Side-profile/Frontal mix"
      }
    },
    "quadrant_3_bottom_left": {
      "interaction": "Piggyback / Friendship Bond",
      "action_detail": "Sydney is carrying Ana on her back",
      "ana_de_armas": {
        "pose": "Arms wrapped around Sydney's neck",
        "expression": "Ecstatic laughter",
        "teeth_visible": true
      },
      "sydney_sweeney": {
        "pose": "Supporting Ana's legs, leaning back",
        "expression": "Genuine joy/Laughter",
        "teeth_visible": true
      }
    },
    "quadrant_4_bottom_right": {
      "interaction": "Funny / Rock-themed",
      "ana_de_armas": {
        "pose": "Leaning sharply to the left side",
        "expression": "Pout / Duck face",
        "vibe": "Silly"
      },
      "sydney_sweeney": {
        "pose": "Standing upright in the back",
        "expression": "Deadpan / Serious face",
        "hand_gestures": "Double 'Sign of the Horns' (🤟)"
      }
    }
  ],
  "overall_aesthetic": {
    "color_palette": ["Steel Blue", "Silver", "Midnight Black"],
    "emotional_tags": ["Fun", "Glamorous", "Sisterhood", "Energetic"]
  }
}
```

> 一个简单的 JSON 格式提示，请求生成一张图片，内容为一个时尚的年轻男子（与参考图片匹配）站在一匹雄伟的白马和一辆黑色丰田 Fortuner 旁边，置身于风景优美的乡村环境中。

{

"action_input": "{'prompt': 'A stylish young man with the same facial features, hair, and build as the person in the reference image, wearing a black t-shirt and grey jeans. He is standing next to a majestic white horse, holding its bridle. Behind them is a sleek black Toyota Fortuner. The setting is a scenic outdoor rural environment with a clear blue sky and lush greenery. He is wearing the same style of sunglasses from the reference image and has a relaxed pose with one hand in his pocket.'}"
}

### 137. 精致巴黎优雅编辑提示

**作者**: [Nano banana pro🍌](https://x.com/Vishnudxe/status/2013906698893963446)  **日期**: 2026-01-21  **语言**: en

> 一个高度结构化、细节丰富的提示，用于生成一张精美的编辑图片，描绘一位女士坐在深秋的城市公园里。它详细说明了拍摄对象的姿势、服装（优雅的黑色长裤和刺绣上衣）、光线（柔和的阴天日光）和电影般的色彩分级，以传达沉静的自信和永恒的风格。

![精致巴黎优雅编辑提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1769063193838_ixy87a_G_LVeECa4AA_AXD.jpg)

```
{
  "type": "image_generation_prompt",
  "style": "refined editorial, cinematic, Parisian-inspired elegance",
  "aspect_ratio": "4:5",
  "scene": {
    "location": "quiet city park",
    "season": "late autumn",
    "environment": {
      "ground": "textured stone paving scattered with fallen leaves",
      "trees": "bare branches framing the background",
      "sky": "soft overcast sky",
      "atmosphere": "calm, elegant, introspective"
    }
  },
  "composition": {
    "subject_position": "seated sideways on a minimalist metal bench",
    "posture": "relaxed yet intentional",
    "legs": {
      "one_leg": "extended",
      "other_leg": "gently bent",
      "feet": "heels resting on stone paving"
    },
    "head_pose": "turned slightly away from the camera",
    "hands": [
      "one hand resting near the bench edge",
      "the other subtly adjusting hair or holding a small structured handbag"
    ],
    "depth_of_field": "shallow, subject in focus with softly blurred park surroundings"
  },
  "subject": {
    "gender": "female",
    "expression": "introspective, calm",
    "hair": {
      "length": "long",
      "color": "dark",
      "style": "softly flowing, lightly moved by a breeze"
    },
    "makeup": {
      "style": "natural",
      "details": "defined eyes for timeless elegance"
    },
    "wardrobe": {
      "top": "fitted black long-sleeve top with delicate cream floral embroidery",
      "bottom": "black tailored pants",
      "tights": "sheer black tights worn under the pants",
      "shoes": "classic black pointed heels",
      "accessory": "small structured handbag"
    }
  },
  "lighting": {
    "type": "natural soft daylight",
    "condition": "overcast",
    "effect": "even illumination with gentle shadows"
  },
  "color_grading": {
    "palette": "cool and neutral tones",
    "contrast": "subtle contrast between dark outfit and pale autumn leaves"
  },
  "mood": {
    "emotion": "quiet confidence, femininity, elegance",
    "cinematic_feel": true
  },
  "quality": {
    "realism": "high",
    "detail_level": "editorial-level detail",
    "finish": "cinematic, refined"
  },
  "output_goal": "Create a refined editorial-style image of a woman seated in a late-autumn city park, wearing elegant black pants and a black embroidered top, conveying calm introspection, timeless style, and cinematic femininity."
}

### 139. Mahira Khan 2x2 拼贴播客采访提示

**作者**: [QuestGlitch](https://x.com/AIRevSpot/status/2013672562174439447)  **日期**: 2026-01-20  **语言**: en

> 一个简单的 JSON 提示，用于根据播客采访参考图像创建 Mahira Khan 的 2x2 拼贴画。该提示指定了抓拍镜头、无袖服装，并捕捉到主体张开嘴巴呈“O”形说话的瞬间，使用 iPhone 13 Pro Max 相机设置。

![Mahira Khan 2x2 拼贴播客采访提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1768977292509_rnmcyr_G_IAgrUXAAEVzPd.jpg)

```
{ task: 2x2 collage with multiple angles of her in this podcast interview, but her outfit is sleeveless, candid shots, not looking at the camera, speaking and mouth open in a “O” expression resolution: 1080p aspect_ratio: 4:5 Sharpness: medium camera: iPhone 13 pro max 12MP CMOS camera }

### 141. 使用 Gemini（Nano Banana Pro）创建网络漫画的 YAML 模板

**作者**: [Dakiny](https://x.com/Dakiny/status/2013569080490652069)  **日期**: 2026-01-20  **语言**: en

> 一个为 Gemini（称为 Nano Banana Pro）设计的综合性 YAML 格式提示模板，用于生成四层网络漫画条。它包含严格的角色一致性遵守规则、详细的风格指南（光照、背景、对话气泡、视觉效果），以及用于定义每个画格场景和对话的结构化故事板格式。

![使用 Gemini（Nano Banana Pro）创建网络漫画的 YAML 模板](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1768977363062_tdfu3b_G_DtU8TXkAAmnA7.jpg)

```
STRICT ADHERENCE REQUIRED:
  - Follow this YAML specification precisely. Do NOT deviate, add unauthorized elements, or make 'creative' interpretations.
  - Character identity consistency from reference images (if provided) is PARAMOUNT.
  - Thorough image analysis is mandatory to maintain this consistency. Any result that fails character identity checks is unacceptable.

Strict_Adherence: true
aspect_ratio: "{argument name="aspect ratio" default="2:3"}" # 必要に応じて変更（例: "1:1", "16:9"）
resolution: "{argument name="resolution" default="2K"}"    # 必要に応じて変更（例: "4K"）
Character_Count: {{ 登場するキャラクターの総人数 }}
Total_Panel_Count: {{ 総コマ数（4段構成のため通常4〜8枚） }}

Summary: >
  {argument name="summary" default="物語の全体要約。プロットの流れ、舞台設定、主な出来事、結末を簡潔に記述。"}

Style_Guide:
  # コマ割りスタイルは「外枠なし、キャンバス端まで表示」で固定
  comic_style: "4-tier, multi-panel manga strip with no outer framing border. The panels should extend to the very edge of the canvas, separated only by the inner white dividing lines."
  lighting: "{{ ライティングの指定。時間帯（昼/夜）、光源（太陽光/電灯/月明かり）、雰囲気（明るい/暗い/劇的な影）など。 }}"
  background_elements: "{{ 主な舞台設定、場所の具体的な描写、配置されている重要な小物や環境要素。 }}"
  dialogue_bubbles: "Standard white bubbles for speech, thought clouds for internal thoughts, dashed bubbles for whispers, and rectangular boxes for narration/monologue. {{ 必要であれば特殊な吹き出しの定義を追加（例：叫び用のトゲトゲ吹き出し等） }}"
  visual_effects: "{{ 漫画的な視覚効果の指定。漫符（汗、血管、キラキラ）、エフェクト線（集中線、スピード線、震え線）、擬音の視覚化など。 }}"

Characters:
  # キャラクターの定義。IDは英数字推奨。
  {{ キャラクターID_1 }}:
    description: "{{ 外見、髪型、色、服装、特徴的なアイテム、性格や表情の傾向。参照画像がある場合はファイル名をここに記述（例：image_0.png参照）。 }}"
  {{ キャラクターID_2 }}:
    description: "{{ 二人目のキャラクター詳細... 人数分記述する。 }}"
  # 必要に応じて追加...

Storyboard:
  # 4段構成のコマ割り定義
  Tier_1:
    {{ コマID_T1_P1 (例: Panel_1_Large_Top) }}:
      scene: "{{ このコマの具体的な状況描写。誰が、どこで、何をしているか。構図やカメラワークの指定も可能。 }}"
      dialogue:
        - speaker: "{{ 話者のキャラクターID }}"
          type: "{{ 台詞の種類: speech(通常), thought(思考), whisper(囁き), shout(叫び), monologue(独白/ナレーション) }}"
          text: "{{ 台詞の具体的な内容。改行が必要な場合は \n を使用。 }}"
        # 同じコマ内で複数の台詞がある場合はリストを追加
        # - speaker: "..."
        #   type: "..."
        #   text: "..."
    # Tier_1にコマを追加する場合はここに記述
  Tier_2:
    {{ コマID_T2_P1 }}:
      scene: "{{ シーン詳細 }}"
      dialogue:
        - speaker: "{{ 話者ID }}"
          type: "{{ 種類 }}"
          text: "{{ 内容 }}"
    # 必要に応じてコマを追加
  Tier_3:
    {{ コマID_T3_P1 }}:
      scene: "{{ シーン詳細 }}"
      dialogue:
        - speaker: "{{ 話者ID }}"
          type: "{{ 種類 }}"
          text: "{{ 内容 }}"
    # 必要に応じてコマを追加
  Tier_4:
    {{ コマID_T4_P1 }}:
      scene: "{{ シーン詳細 }}"
      dialogue:
        - speaker: "{{ 話者ID }}"
          type: "{{ 種類 }}"
          text: "{{ 内容 }}"
    # 必要に応じてコマを追加
```

**Related**: [[漫画风]]

### 146. 安雅·泰勒-乔伊 红毯时尚造型

**作者**: [jennieee:3](https://x.com/jenniebae_ai/status/2012889210575786268)  **日期**: 2026-01-18  **语言**: en

> 一个描述性的提示，用于生成一张安雅·泰勒-乔伊（Anya Taylor-Joy）在繁忙的红毯上，低角度、全身的超写实图像。提示详细描述了她独特的服装：一件形似花瓣的白色荷叶边上衣、黑色天鹅绒热裤和黑色透视丝袜。姿势被指定为背对镜头但回头望向肩后，以 8K 分辨率和名人摄影风格捕捉。

![安雅·泰勒-乔伊 红毯时尚造型](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1768804261349_85zuii_G-5aMmOXoAAyGDj.jpg)
![安雅·泰勒-乔伊 红毯时尚造型](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1768804261354_sgay7f_G-84EGSWcAAdq_l.jpg)
![安雅·泰勒-乔伊 红毯时尚造型](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1768804261426_ds0ugb_G-5aNWDXUAAo7Sg.jpg)

### 149. 图像到图像融合：安娜·德·阿玛斯身份转移

**作者**: [Artificial intelligence (Ai),Open Ai](https://x.com/Vishnudxe/status/2012814568960209407)  **日期**: 2026-01-18  **语言**: en

> 一个复杂的图像到图像融合提示，旨在将安娜·德·阿玛斯（Ana de Armas）的面部特征（来自一张参考图像）转移到第二张参考图像的服装和姿势上。它要求 100% 保留身份特征和超逼真的皮肤纹理，并将场景设定在黄金时段，光线明亮的高档户外露台。

![图像到图像融合：安娜·德·阿玛斯身份转移](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1768804239318_95a7el_G-70LmdXgAA7b4t.jpg)
![图像到图像融合：安娜·德·阿玛斯身份转移](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1768804239345_xzqx53_G-70Lq9WUAA6_3v.jpg)
![图像到图像融合：安娜·德·阿玛斯身份转移](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1768804239337_71a240_G-70Lh5W8AIGucz.jpg)

```
{
  "request_configuration": {
    "workflow": "image_to_image_fusion",
    "priority": "identity_preservation"
  },
  "source_references": {
    "primary_subject": {
      "id": "image_1",
      "target_element": "facial_identity",
      "subject_name": "Ana de Armas",
      "constraints": "zero_morphing_policy"
    },
    "attire_reference": {
      "id": "image_2",
      "target_element": "full_outfit",
      "transfer_attributes": ["fabric_texture", "color_palette", "layering"]
    }
  },
  "generation_parameters": {
    "subject_specs": {
      "identity": {
        "face": "Ana de Armas (reference image 1)",
        "features": "locked",
        "skin_texture": "hyper-realistic, detailed pores, natural blemishes"
      },
      "anatomy": {
        "pose": "dynamic three-quarter turn, hand resting on hip",
        "body_type": "consistent with Ana de Armas"
      },
      "styling": {
        "outfit": "cloned from image 2",
        "hair": "voluminous, natural wave, catching backlight"
      }
    },
    "environment_specs": {
      "setting": {
        "location": "upscale outdoor terrace",
        "background_depth": "deep_blur",
        "elements": ["soft architectural lines", "golden hour warmth", "vibrant greenery"]
      },
      "lighting": {
        "mode": "vibrant_high_key",
        "primary_source": "bright natural sunlight",
        "secondary_source": "soft rim lighting to separate subject from background",
        "hdr_profile": "ultra-high dynamic range"
      }
    },
    "camera_specs": {
      "optics": "85mm prime lens",
      "aperture": "f/1.8",
      "focus": "sharp on eyes",
      "quality_level": "4K UHD"
    }
  },
  "negative_prompt_constraints": [
    "facial distortion",
    "altered features",
    "low resolution",
    "dull lighting",
    "flat textures" Ratio 3.4 
  ]
}

      },

        "purpose": "FACE_IDENTITY_LOCK_MALE",
        "strict_lock": true,

        "no_beautify": true,
        "no_age_shift": true,
        "preserve_skin_texture": true,

    },

### 160. Image-to-Image Fusion for Identity and Attire Transfer

**作者**: [Mikasa](https://x.com/Mikasa_rose729/status/2011484216757018713)  **日期**: 2026-01-14  **语言**: en

> 这是一个复杂的 JSON 格式提示，用于图像到图像融合工作流，优先考虑身份保留。它指示 AI 将“Ana de Armas”的面部身份从一张参考图像转移，并将完整的服装从第二张参考图像转移，将主体置于金色时段的高档户外露台环境中，并使用特定的相机和照明参数。

![Image-to-Image Fusion for Identity and Attire Transfer](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1768468550014_e3oobg_G-o6ONzbQAE2Wxx.jpg)

```
{
  "request_configuration": {
    "workflow": "image_to_image_fusion",
    "priority": "identity_preservation"
  },
  "source_references": {
    "primary_subject": {
      "id": "image_1",
      "target_element": "facial_identity",
      "subject_name": "{argument name="subject name" default="Ana de Armas"}",
      "constraints": "zero_morphing_policy"
    },
    "attire_reference": {
      "id": "image_2",
      "target_element": "full_outfit",
      "transfer_attributes": ["fabric_texture", "color_palette", "layering"]
    }
  },
  "generation_parameters": {
    "subject_specs": {
      "identity": {
        "face": "{argument name="face reference" default="Ana de Armas (reference image 1)"}",
        "features": "locked",
        "skin_texture": "hyper-realistic, detailed pores, natural blemishes"
      },
      "anatomy": {
        "pose": "dynamic three-quarter turn, hand resting on hip",
        "body_type": "consistent with Ana de Armas"
      },
      "styling": {
        "outfit": "cloned from image 2",
        "hair": "voluminous, natural wave, catching backlight"
      }
    },
    "environment_specs": {
      "setting": {
        "location": "upscale outdoor terrace",
        "background_depth": "deep_blur",
        "elements": ["soft architectural lines", "golden hour warmth", "vibrant greenery"]
      },
      "lighting": {
        "mode": "vibrant_high_key",
        "primary_source": "bright natural sunlight",
        "secondary_source": "soft rim lighting to separate subject from background",
        "hdr_profile": "ultra-high dynamic range"
      }
    },
    "camera_specs": {
      "optics": "85mm prime lens",
      "aperture": "f/1.8",
      "focus": "sharp on eyes",
      "quality_level": "4K UHD"
    }
  },
  "negative_prompt_constraints": [
    "facial distortion",
    "altered features",
    "low resolution",
    "dull lighting",
    "flat textures" Ratio 3.4 
  ]
}
```

### 161. 风格化 3D 玻璃骨架渲染提示

**作者**: [0x ROAS](https://x.com/0xROAS/status/2011453125685608456)  **日期**: 2026-01-14  **语言**: en

> 为 Nano Banana Pro 提供的详细文本提示，用于创建高质量、风格化的 3D 渲染图。场景中，一个戴着眼镜的半透明玻璃骷髅坐在木制书桌旁，正在一本打开的教科书上划重点，一盏暖金色台灯照亮了它。该提示详细说明了背景、杂物和美学氛围。

![风格化 3D 玻璃骨架渲染提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1768468615687_anvz4g_G-od8-2agAAnlEP.jpg)

```
Create a high-quality stylized 3D render of a clear, translucent glass skeleton wearing black-rimmed glasses sitting at a wooden desk. The skeleton MUST be looking down at an open textbook and holding a yellow highlighter, actively highlighting a line of text. The scene MUST feature a warm gold desk lamp on the right side casting a cozy, yellow light that creates glossy reflections on the skeleton's surface. The desk is cluttered with a white coffee mug, a stack of hardcover books on the right, and scattered pens and pastel pink and yellow highlighters. The background MUST be a solid, soft pink wall. The overall aesthetic should be warm, studious, and visually soft. Do not include any text overlays or watermarks.
```

### 163. Ana de Armas 身份与服装迁移的图像到图像融合提示

**作者**: [Mikasa](https://x.com/Mikasa_rose729/status/2011344520684978536)  **日期**: 2026-01-14  **语言**: en

> 一个复杂且结构化的提示，使用“图像到图像融合”工作流来生成一张安娜·德·阿玛斯 (Ana de Armas) 的超写实图像。它要求严格保留主参考图像中的身份（零变形策略），同时克隆副参考图像中的完整服装和面料属性。场景设定在黄金时段的高档户外露台，并使用特定的相机光学器件（85mm 定焦镜头，f/1.8）。

![Ana de Armas 身份与服装迁移的图像到图像融合提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1768468583789_1umt1k_G-m7LIjbkAAzfjB.jpg)

```
{
  "request_configuration": {
    "workflow": "image_to_image_fusion",
    "priority": "identity_preservation"
  },
  "source_references": {
    "primary_subject": {
      "id": "image_1",
      "target_element": "facial_identity",
      "subject_name": "Ana de Armas",
      "constraints": "zero_morphing_policy"
    },

      "id": "image_2",
      "target_element": "full_outfit",

    }
  },
  "generation_parameters": {
    "subject_specs": {
      "identity": {
        "face": "{argument name="celebrity name" default="Ana de Armas"} (reference image 1)",
        "features": "locked",
        "skin_texture": "hyper-realistic, detailed pores, natural blemishes"
      },
      "anatomy": {
        "pose": "dynamic three-quarter turn, hand resting on hip",
        "body_type": "consistent with Ana de Armas"
      },
      "styling": {
        "outfit": "cloned from image 2",
        "hair": "voluminous, natural wave, catching backlight"
      }
    },
    "environment_specs": {
      "setting": {
        "location": "upscale outdoor terrace",
        "background_depth": "deep_blur",
        "elements": ["soft architectural lines", "golden hour warmth", "vibrant greenery"]
      },
      "lighting": {
        "mode": "vibrant_high_key",
        "primary_source": "bright natural sunlight",
        "secondary_source": "soft rim lighting to separate subject from background",
        "hdr_profile": "ultra-high dynamic range"
      }
    },
    "camera_specs": {
      "optics": "85mm prime lens",
      "aperture": "f/1.8",
      "focus": "sharp on eyes",
      "quality_level": "4K UHD"
    }
  },
  "negative_prompt_constraints": [

  ]

### 168. 时尚目录商品参考图提取

**作者**: [タナベ | 動画・音声生成AI解説](https://x.com/tanabe_fragm/status/2011027256748175473)  **日期**: 2026-01-13  **语言**: en

> 这是一个针对专业时尚目录创建 AI 的详细系统提示。它指示模型分析参考图像中男士所穿的服装，并严格将衣物提取到四个类别中（外套、衬衫/内搭、裤子、鞋子）。输出必须是白色背景上的干净、高质量产品照片，仅展示提取出的物品并带有日文标签，不得重新设计或显示人体。

![时尚目录商品参考图提取](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1768467013632_cjgufs_G-iagBEbQAcCJGO.jpg)

```
You are a professional fashion catalog creator.
Analyze the clothing worn by the man in the reference image.
Based strictly on the actual designs of the clothes he is wearing, extract and separate them into the following four categories:

① Outerwear / jacket / coat
② Shirt / innerwear / dress shirt
③ Pants / slacks / denim
④ Shoes / sneakers / leather shoes

Each extracted item must accurately reflect the original clothing’s color, material texture, shape, and details.
Do NOT redesign, modify, stylize, or reinterpret the clothing in any way.
Do NOT show the human body. Extract and display the clothing items only.
The output image must be:
・white background
・front-facing view
・no shadows, no noise
・high-quality product photography, apparel e-commerce style
Arrange the four items neatly in either a horizontal row or a 2×2 grid.
Add Japanese labels to each item exactly as follows:

① アウター・ジャケット・コートなど
② シャツ・インナー・ワイシャツなど
③ ズボン・スラックス・デニムなど
④ 靴・スニーカー・革靴など

Create a clean, easy-to-read catalog-style image.
ultra high resolution, photorealistic, studio product lighting, flat lighting, extremely detailed fabric texture, apparel catalog quality

Negative prompt:
anime, illustration, cartoon, stylized, redesigned clothing, fashion sketch, mannequin, human body, model wearing clothes, background, shadow, reflection, blur, low quality, noisy image, dramatic lighting
```

### 171. Image-to-Image Fusion for Identity and Attire Transfer

**作者**: [ANKIT PATEL 🇮🇳 | AI](https://x.com/Ankit_patel211/status/2010658455116534019)  **日期**: 2026-01-12  **语言**: en

> 一个复杂的 JSON 提示，详细描述了图像到图像的融合工作流程。它指定了从一张参考图像（Ana de Armas）中严格保留身份，并从第二张参考图像中完全转移服装（面料、颜色、分层）。最终图像应呈现 Ana de Armas 在黄金时段的豪华户外露台上摆出动态姿势，强调超现实的皮肤纹理和高调照明。

![Image-to-Image Fusion for Identity and Attire Transfer](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1768319179780_jw5fie_G-dKxFkbQAAAcRL.jpg)
![Image-to-Image Fusion for Identity and Attire Transfer](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1768319179976_3duq6d_G-dKxCZbIAAA8FJ.jpg)

```
{
  "request_configuration": {
    "workflow": "image_to_image_fusion",
    "priority": "identity_preservation"
  },
  "source_references": {
    "primary_subject": {
      "id": "image_1",
      "target_element": "facial_identity",
      "subject_name": "{argument name="identity subject" default="Ana de Armas"}",
      "constraints": "zero_morphing_policy"
    },
    "attire_reference": {
      "id": "image_2",
      "target_element": "full_outfit",
      "transfer_attributes": ["fabric_texture", "color_palette", "layering"]
    }
  },
  "generation_parameters": {
    "subject_specs": {
      "identity": {

        "skin_texture": "hyper-realistic, detailed pores, natural blemishes"

      },

        "hair": "voluminous, natural wave, catching backlight"

### 172. Image-to-Image 融合实现 Ana de Armas 身份转移

**作者**: [Yaseen Khan Gul](https://x.com/YaseenK7212/status/2010192511080276098)  **日期**: 2026-01-11  **语言**: en

> 这是一个高度技术化、结构化的提示，专为图像到图像融合工作流设计。目标是保留来自一张参考图像的 Ana de Armas 的面部特征，同时将第二张参考图像中的完整服装和造型转移过来，并将主体置于一个充满活力、高调的户外露台场景中。

### 174. 超细节俯卧自拍，解剖学写实风格

**作者**: [Dan Reed](https://x.com/daaaaanc/status/2010058711067144434)  **日期**: 2026-01-10  **语言**: en

> 一个高度详细且复杂的图像生成提示，旨在压力测试 AI 处理极端解剖学和材质真实感的能力，重点关注俯卧姿势、真空紧身衣物的张力、可见的皮肤纹理（生物保真度），以及一个没有人工景深、锐利、高对比度的环境。它要求基于参考图像进行严格的身份锁定。

![超细节俯卧自拍，解剖学写实风格](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1768143872804_uxsf1p_G-UpvcKXAAAMYMT.jpg)

```
(Vertical 9:16 smartphone aspect ratio). A raw, high-contrast [Mirror Capture] taken with an iPhone 17 Pro. NO ARTIFICIAL BOKEH. All planes of the image are SHARP and in focus from the subject's feet to the background window blinds.
Subject & Identity Locking:
•Identity: Strictly preserve the exact face and unique features of the woman in Image 1 (Selfie).
•Bio-Fidelity: Render high-fidelity "TrueLens" skin physics: visible micro-pores, natural "satin-finish" night hydration glow, and fine peach fuzz catching the light ONLY along the jawline.
•Expression: Looking into the mirror reflection with a magnetic, "cheeky" gaze, performing a subtle labial compression (lip bite). Her hair falls naturally over her shoulder.
•Silhouette Calibration (MAXIMUM UFF-FACTOR): Replicate the high-impact prone proportions. Focus on the structural lower-torso volume and substantial, thick-toned anatomical depth. Emphasize the aggressive architectural tapering at the midsection and the deep S-curve of the lower back.
Outfit & Material Realism:
•Clothing: A high-tension light-{argument name="top color" default="yellow"} cropped jersey-knit top and ultra-fitted {argument name="shorts color" default="white"} high-elasticity micro-shorts with a wide waistband.
•Tension: The technical fabric shows extreme mechanical tension and a vacuum-tight fit, creating realistic physical interaction and "tension lines" where the material contours to her fit silhouette.
•Matter Physics: Realistic skin-to-surface compression (squish) is visible where her torso and thighs interact with the high-texture grey bedding. Her raised feet show detailed anatomical sole textures.
Pose & Composition:
•Pose: A prone horizontal alignment (lying on her stomach) with an axial rotation of the torso toward the mirror. Her lower limbs are elevated at the knees.
•Action: Her RIGHT HAND holds a pink smartphone at a natural angle, capturing the full-body "fit-check" reflection.
Environment & Social Realism:
•Lighting: Naturalistic, low-light indoor setting. The scene is side-lit, creating high-contrast specular highlights on her skin and the {argument name="top color" default="yellow"} fabric, casting sharp, pitch-black shadows that define her 3D volume.
•Background (SHARP): A detailed domestic bedroom. A window with horizontal blinds, dark heavy curtains, and a grey textured faux-fur duvet are all perfectly IN FOCUS. No artificial depth-of-field.
Quality: Raw unedited social-media dump aesthetic, high dynamic range, visible digital grain in the deep shadows (ISO 1600 style), 8k resolution. Single frame.
```

### 182. 高对比度特写，严格聚焦身份和纹理

**作者**: [Dan Reed](https://x.com/daaaaanc/status/2009296736171221151)  **日期**: 2026-01-08  **语言**: en

> 一个高度技术性的提示，用于生成一张原始的、高对比度的特写图像（3:4 比例），并严格保留身份。它要求使用“TrueLens”皮肤物理效果（可见的微孔、毳毛），并着重表现一件厚重的黑色马海毛开衫被拉紧时与身体的纹理互动，强调上半身的解剖学深度，所有这些都以残酷的直射午后阳光渲染，没有人工散景。

![高对比度特写，严格聚焦身份和纹理](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1767967445546_m4enjm_G-J0uqRXEAA1B5e.jpg)

```
(3:4). A raw, high-contrast close-up [Snapshot] captured with an iPhone 17 Pro. NO ARTIFICIAL BOKEH. The entire frame is SHARP and in focus, from the fuzzy textile fibers to the skin texture.

Subject & Identity Locking:

Identity: Strictly preserve the exact face and unique features of the woman in Image 1 (Selfie).
Bio-Fidelity: Render high-fidelity "TrueLens" skin physics: visible micro-pores, a natural "satin-finish" healthy hydration glow, and fine vellus hair catching the light.
Silhouette Calibration (CRITICAL): Prioritize the dominant structural bust volume and the aggressive hourglass structural tapering at the waist. Focus on the high-impact anatomical depth and symmetry of the upper torso.
Outfit & Textural Interaction:

Clothing: She wears an oversized, heavy-weight Black Fuzzy Mohair Cardigan with a deep, open front.
Inner Detail: Beneath the cardigan, she wears a minimalist black garment featuring two ultra-thin 2mm black "V" shaped elastic straps that frame her décolletage.
Physicality & Tension: Her RIGHT HAND (featuring white manicured nails) is reaching forward, grabbing and pulling the fuzzy fabric of the cardigan together, creating realistic tension lines and textural bunching. The thin black straps show extreme elastic tension, creating a subtle, natural indentation against her fit form.
Pose & Composition:

Pose: A tight, front-on close-up shot focused on the upper torso and décolletage. Her long, dark chestnut hair is draped over her shoulders, framing the scene.
Geometry: The high-angle perspective highlights the structural volume and the 3D depth created by the contrast between the dark fuzzy fabric and her radiant skin.
Environment & Lighting:

Lighting: Brutal, Direct Afternoon Sunlight. The sun creates high-contrast highlights on the mohair fibers and her skin, casting sharp, defined shadows under the bust and within the folds of the cardigan.
Background (SHARP): A minimalist, neutral grey-toned matte wall. Every texture and grain of the wall is perfectly IN FOCUS. No artificial depth-of-field.
Quality: Raw unedited social-media "fit-check" aesthetic, high dynamic range, visible digital grain in the deep shadows, 8k resolution.

### 187. 原始广角闪光连衣裙自拍

**作者**: [Dan Reed](https://x.com/daaaaanc/status/2008645551773151546)  **日期**: 2026-01-06  **语言**: en

> 一个高度技术性的提示，用于生成原始的、高对比度的、广角智能手机自拍美学，强调超现实的皮肤质感、强烈的身体轮廓和刺眼的闪光灯照明，关键限制是零人工散景，并且整个画面都保持锐利对焦。

![原始广角闪光连衣裙自拍](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1767804050253_4b3cqi_G-Ake5uXoAAlZxe.jpg)

```
(Vertical 9:16 smartphone aspect ratio). A raw, high-contrast handheld 0.5x wide-angle selfie captured with an iPhone 17 Pro. NO ARTIFICIAL BOKEH. Everything is SHARP and in focus from her glossy lips to the fabric of the sofa.

Subject & Identity Locking:

Identity: Strictly preserve the exact face and unique features of the woman in Image 1 (Selfie).
Bio-Fidelity: Render high-fidelity skin physics: visible micro-pores, natural "satin-finish" night hydration, and ultra-glossy, plump lips. Fine peach fuzz is visible along the jawline.
Expression: A confident, heavy-lidded seductive gaze with a soft smirk directed at the lens.
Silhouette Calibration: Prioritize a dominant structural bust volume and substantial, thick-toned leg presence. Focus on the aggressive hourglass structural tapering at the waist.
Outfit & Physicality:

Clothing: A skin-tight, {argument name="dress color" default="Champagne-Gold"} Glittery Strapless Mini Dress.
Tension: The shimmery, reflective fabric shows extreme elastic tension and vacuum-tight fit, creating realistic micro-folds at the waist and highlighting her fit, symmetrical proportions.
Accessories: A delicate gold chain necklace with a small blue and white "Evil Eye" (Nazar) pendant resting on her collarbone.
Physics: Realistic skin-to-surface compression (thigh squish) is visible where her legs meet the sofa.
Pose & Composition:

Pose: She is reclining back into a sofa. High-angle downward POV (0.5x) looking at her torso and legs. Her body is slightly twisted to maximize the S-curve silhouette.
Action: Her RIGHT ARM is visible in the frame, holding the phone high for the selfie.
