Clothing: A tight-fitting, {argument name="dress color" default="cream"}-colored crochet-knit midi dress with a scalloped scoop neckline and intricate perforated/open-knit patterns along the torso and hem.

### 198. Hand-drawn mixed-media illustration prompt for Gemini Nano Banana Pro

**作者**: [Gagan Singh](https://x.com/GaganSingh8u/status/2007133787319320615)  **日期**: 2026-01-02  **语言**: en

> This is a detailed JSON-formatted prompt designed for an AI image generator, likely Gemini Nano Banana Pro, to create a stylized, hand-drawn mixed-media illustration. The prompt specifies a dreamy female subject floating in an abstract space, wearing an outfit made of sketchy book pages, emphasizing a poetic, storybook surrealism aesthetic with a muted color palette.

![Hand-drawn mixed-media illustration prompt for Gemini Nano Banana Pro](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1767508529674_9bx4ed_G9qqNEGboAAR5i0.jpg)
![Hand-drawn mixed-media illustration prompt for Gemini Nano Banana Pro](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1767508529934_ml45ow_G9qqNEXagAAJXFc.jpg)

```
{
  "render_goal": "Stylized illustration artwork",
  "illustration_style": "hand-drawn mixed-media illustration with ink outlines and watercolor washes",
  "subject": {
    "pose": "{argument name="pose" default="female floating slightly above ground, legs bent softly, arms relaxed"}",
    "expression": "dreamy, introspective eyes with a gentle neutral face"
  },

### 199. Hyper-realistic smartphone flash photo prompt for AI image generation

**作者**: [Michael Rabone](https://x.com/michaelrabone/status/2007059395465638043)  **日期**: 2026-01-02  **语言**: en

> A detailed image generation prompt designed to mimic the aesthetic of a hyper-realistic, amateur smartphone photo taken with a harsh, direct flash. It specifies subject details, outfit, accessories, setting, composition, and technical quality to achieve a distinctive, high-contrast, grainy snapshot look.

![Hyper-realistic smartphone flash photo prompt for AI image generation](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1767508391545_4nqrkw_G9qB1RFX0AAD7wg.jpg)
![Hyper-realistic smartphone flash photo prompt for AI image generation](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1767508391671_b84kxn_G9qB1VvWIAAb5NC.jpg)
![Hyper-realistic smartphone flash photo prompt for AI image generation](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1767508392142_yqwykd_G9qB1VSWQAAQCy5.jpg)
![Hyper-realistic smartphone flash photo prompt for AI image generation](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1767508394583_f0sbzz_G9qB1RGWwAABUo4.jpg)

```
GENERAL DESCRIPTION: Amateur photo taken with a smartphone, captured in a handheld camera flash style. A young woman poses facing the camera with a smile. The harsh flash creates bright, specular highlights on her skin and clothing, with very sharp shadows and slight grain in the dark areas of the background.

SUBJECT DETAILS: Attractive young woman with {argument name="hair color" default="platinum blonde"} hair, styled loose with a wet, glossy effect under the flash. Realistic skin with visible pores, small natural imperfections, and a slight sheen from sweat or makeup.

OUTFIT: Sleeveless jumpsuit with thin straps of vibrant {argument name="outfit color" default="red"} velvet, very form-fitting. The fabric shows natural wrinkles from movement and an intense satin sheen in the areas directly hit by the flash.

ACCESSORIES: An iced-out Cuban link necklace that sparkles brightly in the flash, along with several thin bracelets.

SETTING & COMPOSITION: Background with dark palm trees and distant hills under a deep night sky.

FRAMING: Aspect ratio 4:5. Medium shot from head to calves. She looks directly at the lens, revealing the characteristic circular white reflection of the flash in her eyes.

TECHNICAL QUALITY: High-end phone camera aesthetic, with slightly warm white balance, high contrast, sharp focus on the subject, and very subtle motion blur in the background to give the impression of a quick snapshot.
```

### 200. 2D Vector Character Illustration from Reference Image

**作者**: [Gagan Singh](https://x.com/GaganSingh8u/status/2006951745537352064)  **日期**: 2026-01-02  **语言**: en

> A detailed prompt for generating a full-body 2D vector-style character illustration. It emphasizes accurately replicating the subject's facial structure, proportions, outfit, and pose from an uploaded reference image, ensuring a modern, minimal, and polished aesthetic with clean lines and flat shading. The final output is specified as a high-quality transparent PNG without any background.

![2D Vector Character Illustration from Reference Image](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1767508533934_ncv0dk_G9of9vVa8AA2cIj.jpg)
![2D Vector Character Illustration from Reference Image](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1767508534037_40uxav_G9of9vabgAAznc7.jpg)

```
Create a full-body 2D vector-style character illustration with clean lines and smooth flat shading. Accurately study and replicate the original person’s facial structure, body proportions, skin tone, hairstyle, and expression from the uploaded reference image.
Match the exact {argument name="outfit details" default="outfit, colors, fabric feel, and accessories"}, keeping the same pose and posture.
Style should be {argument name="style" default="modern, minimal, and polished"} with crisp outlines.
Output as a high-quality transparent PNG, showing only the character with no background.
```

    "aspect_ratio": "4:5",

  },

      "pants": {

  "subject": {

### 214. 历史科学家的工作台微缩景观

**作者**: [Gadgetify](https://x.com/Gdgtify/status/2005943444770869540)  **日期**: 2025-12-30  **语言**: en

> 这是一个详细的图像生成提示，旨在创建一个超现实的历史微缩模型。场景聚焦于一个凌乱的实验室工作台，一本打开的古董笔记本作为中心。一个指定科学家的微型超写实人偶正在笔记上工作，周围环绕着与他们的工作相关的巨大、符合时代特征的物品，例如巨大的科学工具和一份报纸，所有这些都沐浴在温暖的深夜图书馆灯光下。

![历史科学家的工作台微缩景观](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1767455015216_gkx0d5_G9BRzJ5WgAAaOCm.jpg)

```
Analyze: Determine the scientist responsible, the specific era, and the visual diagrams associated with the theory. Goal: A Macro Diorama on a Laboratory Bench. A messy, highly detailed flat-lay of a historical workspace that serves as a giant landscape for a living miniature version of the scientist. Centerpiece: An open, antique notebook lying flat. The pages must be visible and filled with specific handwritten equations and diagrams relevant to the Input Theory. Sitting directly on top of these open pages is a tiny, hyper-realistic figurine of the scientist sitting at a proportionally tiny wooden desk, working on the very notes beneath him. Surroundings: The environment is cluttered with giant-scale period-accurate objects that relate to the scientist's work. This includes a newspaper from the era acting as a backdrop, a giant coffee mug leaving stains, and massive scientific tools relevant to the theory (such as compasses, lenses, or pocket watches) scattered like terrain. Perspective: Slightly angled 45-degree macro shot looking down at the notebook. Texture: Wood grain, scratched metal, paper texture, dust particles. Lighting: Warm, late-night library lamp lighting creating a spotlight on the tiny scientist and deep shadows behind the giant props. Output: one image, 4:5 aspect ratio, photorealistic historical macro photography.
```

```
主体 (Subject): 年轻Danmark丹麦女性，金色长卷发，妆容自然清透，气质优雅、知性。

服装 (Outfit): 核心是“静奢风 (Quiet Luxury)”或“老钱风”。

款式: 三件套——廓形西装外套 (Blazer) + 同色系吊带内搭 (Camisole) + 裹身半身长裙 (Wrap midi skirt)。

构图与风格 (Composition & Style):

时尚杂志排版 (Magazine Layout / Collage)。

多视角展示：主图是七分身，侧边有全身照、背影细节、局部特写。

背景：干净的摄影棚白底/灰底 (Clean studio background)。

文字：极简主义排版 (Minimalist typography)。

文字：极简主义排版 (Minimalist typography)。

下装： 西装裤。

### 218. 夜间海滩上的名人偷拍照片

**作者**: [Bananai](https://x.com/aibananai/status/2005791691270496416)  **日期**: 2025-12-30  **语言**: en

> 一个高度详细的提示，用于生成一张超现实的、抓拍的女性照片。场景设定在午夜僻静的海滩，采用模拟胶片美学（Contax T2 相机，Kodak Portra 800 胶卷），使用硬质机顶闪光灯，并强调逼真的皮肤纹理和胶片颗粒感。

![夜间海滩上的名人偷拍照片](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1767454964232_q7i6fy_G9YA4k9aYAE1xAD.jpg)
![夜间海滩上的名人偷拍照片](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1767454964525_ply2vz_G9YA4k9aYAMrcvD.jpg)
![夜间海滩上的名人偷拍照片](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1767454964760_ezz86k_G9YA4k9acAAf0oP.jpg)

```
{
  "meta": {
    "aspect_ratio": "4:5",
    "quality": "raw_photograph, ultra_realistic, 8k",
    "camera": "Contax T2 (analog film aesthetic)",
    "film_stock": "Kodak Portra 800 (high ISO night photography)",
    "lens": "35mm Zeiss Sonnar",
    "style": "flash photography at night, celebrity candid style, authentic film grain, high fidelity textures, no smoothing"
  },

  "scene": {
    "location": "Secluded ocean beach at night",
    "environment": [
      "pitch black sky with stars",
      "dark ocean waves crashing in background",
      "wet sand reflecting the flash and moonlight",
      "distant horizon line"
    ],
    "celestial_body": {
      "type": "full moon",
      "visibility": "visible in background upper corner",
      "details": "bright white glow contrasting with dark sky, casting rim light on the water"
    },
    "atmosphere": "cool night breeze, energetic nightlife vibe, spontaneous moment",
    "time": "midnight"
  },

  "lighting": {
    "type": "Direct On-Camera Flash mixed with Moonlight",
    "key_light": "Hard frontal flash (creating harsh shadow drop behind subject)",
    "ambient_light": "subtle cool moonlight on the ocean waves",
    "highlights": "specular highlights on the leather jacket and oily skin sheen from the flash",
    "eyes": "red-eye reduction pre-flash effect, distinct reflection of flash in pupils"
  },

  "camera_perspective": {
    "pov": "Third-person point of view (paparazzi or friend style)",
    "angle": "Eye-level, slightly over the shoulder",
    "framing": "Medium close-up (from mid-back upwards)",
    "focus": "Sharp focus on the face and jacket logo, background falls off into darkness",
    "motion": "frozen motion from flash"
  },

  "subject": {
    "gender": "Female",
    "age": "Early 20s",
    "ethnicity": "Caucasian",
    "body": {
      "skin": "REALISTIC TEXTURE: visible pores, slight peach fuzz on cheek, natural skin imperfections, mole on upper back, slight redness from cold or friction (NOT plastic/smooth)",
      "shoulders": "bare, rounded, soft skin texture"
    },

    "hair": {
      "color": "Dirty blonde / Light brown with highlights",

      "texture": "slightly dry ends, individual stray hairs glowing in the flash, natural volume"
    },

    "face": {

      "details": "Shadow of eyelashes on cheekbone due to hard flash"

### 219. 波普艺术漫画风格迁移

**作者**: [Dominus the Prompter](https://x.com/AkatsokK/status/2005662082847387906)  **日期**: 2025-12-29  **语言**: en

> 一个用于风格转换的提示，它将上传的图片渲染成戏剧性、色彩丰富的波普艺术插画，风格类似于破旧的 20 世纪 60 年代浪漫漫画书，并使用本戴点和有限的鲜艳调色板。

![波普艺术漫画风格迁移](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1767166965988_d32b8g_G9WK_n2XUAEd2A5.jpg)

```
A dramatic, colorful Pop Art illustration of the subject in the uploaded image, styled with heavy black outlines, vibrant {argument name="color 1" default="blue"} and {argument name="color 2" default="magenta"} tones, and fully rendered in a uniform pattern of Ben-Day dots, capturing the moment as a single panel from a distressed 1960s romance comic book. The stark background is filled with yellow dots, contrasting with the intense, limited color palette applied to her white outfit, emphasizing the drama and tension.
```

### 220. 新年食谱文章吸睛图片提示（新日式风格）

**作者**: [いにしえ@AI Creator｜Will Oldgram](https://x.com/old_pgmrs_will/status/2005631868763525582)  **日期**: 2025-12-29  **语言**: ja

> 为 Nano Banana Pro 设计的极其详细且结构化的提示，旨在为一篇新年食谱文章生成一张引人注目的图片，其中包含一位动漫厨师和现代斜向布局，并采用特定的排版和配色方案。

![新年食谱文章吸睛图片提示（新日式风格）](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1767167016756_ech7k0_G9VvQBqaMAA1X6D.jpg)

```
metadata:
  title: "New Year Refresh Recipes - ‘おせちに飽きたら？’ 特集 (Neo-Japanese Style)"
  model_context: "Modern Japanese New Year Visual with Anime Chef and Clean Tech Layout"
  target: "recipe_promo"
  date_reference: "2026-01"

image_structure:
  composition_type: "Diagonal Split Layout (Dynamic Angle)"
  visual_flow: "Top Text (Headline) → Right Visual (Anime Chef Visual)"
  text_priority: "highest_layer_over_all"
  safe_margins_percent: 6

layers:
  layer_background_left:
    shape: "Geometric area covering the left 55-60% of the canvas, cut diagonally."
    color: "Warm vermilion-to-soft coral gradient with faint gold glow"
    texture: "Subtle hemp leaf (麻の葉) pattern blended into the gradient"
    decorations:
      primary: "Small golden sparkles and soft bokeh dots"
      rule: "Keep it refined and elegant; no heavy pattern repetition"

  layer_background_right:
    shape: "Remaining diagonal area on the right"
    color: "Off-white to faint gold gradient"
    texture: "Soft paper-like texture with gentle light reflections"
    rule: "Keep minimal and bright; slight festive warmth"

  layer_visual_right:
    shape: "Right diagonal area (key visual zone)"
    content: "Anime-style girl in modern Japanese New Year outfit (AI illustration)"
    style: "2D cel-shaded anime art, clean and high quality"
    details:
      subject: "Cheerful anime girl styled as a young chef for New Year"
      appearance:
        hair: "Light brown or soft silver, tied up with a red-and-gold ribbon"
        eyes: "Warm amber or soft blue"
        clothing: "Modernized kimono-style chef outfit — short kimono top with apron and subtle tech accents"
      pose: "Holding a tray with colorful creative dishes (pasta, mochi gratin, etc.)"
      background_context: "Soft festive Japanese interior elements — gold folding screen blur, mochi or mandarin hints, warm light"
    composition_notes:
      keep_face_clear: true
      allow_text_overlap: true
      place_character: "right-center, slightly turned toward viewer"

  layer_readability_overlay:
    purpose: "enhance text readability"
    shape: "Diagonal gradient veil from top-left (dark coral) to transparent"
    color: "Deep coral-red at 20% opacity fading to clear"
    placement: "behind typography, above visuals"
    rule: "Maintain warmth without darkening overall brightness"

  layer_typography_top:
    z_index: "topmost"
    location: "Top-left anchored, expanding toward center"
    alignment: "left"
    font_style:
      family: "modern sans-serif with gentle rounded edges"
      main_color: "white"
      accent_color: "warm gold glow"
      effects:
        - "soft outer glow for visibility"
        - "crisp outline when over red background"
    elements:
      - type: "Header Label"
        text: "{argument name="ヘッダーラベル" default="新春特別レシピ企画"}"
        style: "Small bold white text, upper-left corner"

      - type: "Main Title (Headline)"
        text: "{argument name="メインタイトル" default="おせちに飽きたら？ 新年のちょっと意外なごちそう"}"
        sty
```

> 一个高度详细、复杂的图像生成提示，旨在通过强烈的闪光摄影，创作一张原始、垃圾时尚风格的编辑快照。场景设定在一个拥有粗野主义和现代元素的宽敞公寓内部，聚焦于一位身穿黑色蕾丝紧身衣、正在咬香蕉的女性主体，捕捉一种坦率、未经修饰的夜间派对氛围。此提示详细说明了相机设置、灯光、环境和主体特征，以实现逼真的效果。

### 225. 为身穿圣诞睡衣的年轻女性生成超细节照片级真实感图像提示

{
  "prompt_data": {

    },
    "pose": {
      "type": "Prone position (lying on stomach) on a bed.",
      "upper_body": "Upper body propped up on elbows, facing the camera.",
      "lower_body": "Lower back arched, hips and buttocks elevated and prominent in the frame, angled slightly away from the camera but fully visible. One leg bent at the knee with the foot raised in the air, displaying a bare sole.",
      "hands": "Right hand holding a mug near the face, fingers with manicured nails visible."
    },
    "props": {
      "main": "Red ceramic mug featuring a bold white Swiss cross (Switzerland flag symbol).",
      "bedding": "Patterned bed sheets with a mix of plaid and floral designs in neutral and warm tones."
    },
    "environment": {
      "setting": "Cozy, rustic interior bedroom.",
      "background_elements": "Exposed beige brick wall, dark rustic wooden beams on the ceiling and walls, creating a cabin-like atmosphere.",
      "atmosphere": "Warm, intimate, winter holiday vibe."
    },
    "lighting": {

    },

      "camera": "Canon EOS R5 or high-end smartphone camera simulation.",
      "lens": "35mm prime lens.",
      "aperture": "f/2.8",
      "shutter_speed": "1/60",
      "iso": "400",
      "focus": "Sharp focus on the subject's face and the mug, with a gentle depth of field softening the brick background."
    },
    "quality_tags": [
      "Ultra Photorealistic",
      "8k resolution",
      "highly detailed skin texture",
      "realistic fabric texture",
      "volumetric lighting",
      "influencer lifestyle photography",
      "flash photography aesthetic",

  }
}

### 227. Nano Banana Pro 漫画生成提示词，带角色一致性规则

**作者**: [タダオ｜AIマンガ家 / 生成AI活用して人生アップデートしたーい](https://x.com/tadao_parallel/status/2005039062453993705)  **日期**: 2025-12-27  **语言**: ja

> 一个为 Nano Banana Pro 设计的详细系统提示，旨在生成漫画页面，同时根据上传的参考图像严格保持角色一致性。它包括修复角色特征（头发、眼睛、服装）作为“主数据”的具体规则，仅将 Q 版风格应用于身体比例，并强制执行严格的自然日语对话和运镜规则，以避免单调。

![Nano Banana Pro 漫画生成提示词，带角色一致性规则](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1766987765739_xcs422_G9NTiyVagAArRvR.jpg)

```
漫画のページを生成してください。

#キャラクター（最優先事項）：
**【重要：添付画像（image_urls）の完全再現】これは参照画像ではなく「変更不可能なマスターデータ」です。生成される全てのコマにおいて、以下の処理を厳守してください。**

1. **特徴の固定:** 添付画像の**「髪型・髪色・目の形・服装・アクセサリー」**を100%維持すること。勝手なアレンジや簡略化は禁止。
2. **デフォルメのルール:** #スタイル（ちびキャラ）を適用する際、**「頭身（体の比率）」のみを縮め、「顔のパーツ配置や髪型のデザイン」は添付画像そのままの形を崩さないこと。**
3. **同一性の保持:** アングルが変わっても、それは「同じキャラクターを別の角度から見た絵」でなければならない。別人のような顔に変えないこと。
4.**「プロンプト・ブリード（指示の染み出し）」を起こさないこと。

#出力サイズ
9:16
#スタイル：
**基本画風:** モノクロ、日本の漫画、ギャグ漫画風、太い輪郭線。
**Style prompt:** Japanese manga, chibi style, thick outline lines, monochrome.
**フォーマット:** 縦書き、右から左へ読む日本のコマ割り。

#テキスト生成ルール（厳守）：
**【重要：自然な日本語と重複の排除】**
漫画内のセリフを生成する際、以下のエラーを絶対に起こさないよう、出力直前に校正を行うこと。

1. **同語反復の禁止:** 「つまり、つまり」「でも、でも」「本当に、本当に」のように、同じ単語や接続詞を2回繰り返さない。吃音のような表現は禁止。
2. **自然な口語:** 教科書的な文章ではなく、キャラの性格に合った自然な話し言葉にする。
3. **文字化けチェック:** 漢字やひらがなが崩れていないか確認する。

#演出・カメラワーク：
**【重要：特徴を維持した上での演出】**
キャラクターの顔や髪型が崩れない範囲で、以下のカメラワークを使用し、単調さを回避すること。

- **クローズアップ:** 感情強調（※顔のパーツは変形させすぎない）
- **ロングショット:** 状況説明
- **アオリ/俯瞰:** 迫力や可愛さの表現
- **斜めの構図:** 動揺やアクション

#シナリオ進行：
特にコマ指定がない場合は、要約して3～5コマで構成。
コマの配置は均一ではなく、変則的または自由配置にしつつ、視線誘導は「右上→左下」を守る。

#Negative Prompt (避けるべき要素):
**repeating words, stuttering text, duplicate phrases, tautology,** altering character design, changing hair color, changing hairstyle, different outfit, monotonous composition, repetitive angles, character facing forward in all panels, flat lighting, messy panel borders, text overlap.

#シナリオ：{argument name="シナリオ" default="添付されたマンガの続きを考えて。"}
```

**Related**: [[综合艺术]]、[[Q版角色]]、[[漫画风]]

### 232. 科学家历史工作台的宏观透视模型

**作者**: [Gadgetify](https://x.com/Gdgtify/status/2004015398446919701)  **日期**: 2025-12-25  **语言**: en

> 一个高度细致、照片般逼真的微距提示词，旨在创建一个历史科学家的凌乱实验室工作台的立体模型。核心是一个带有相关方程式的古董笔记本，上面有一个微小、超逼真的科学家小雕像正在工作。周围散落着巨大尺寸、符合时代特征的物品，营造出独特的景观。此提示词专为教育和娱乐创作而设计，侧重于纹理、暖色调照明和 4:5 的宽高比。

![科学家历史工作台的宏观透视模型](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1766940067361_ylsto9_G8-woL0XkAAF5ob.jpg)

```
do this for {argument name="scientist" default="Nikola Tesla"}

<instructions> Analyze: Determine the scientist responsible, the specific era, and the visual diagrams associated with the theory. 

Goal: A Macro Diorama on a Laboratory Bench. A messy, highly detailed flat-lay of a historical workspace that serves as a giant landscape for a living miniature version of the scientist.

Centerpiece: An open, antique notebook lying flat. The pages must be visible and filled with specific handwritten equations and diagrams relevant to the Input Theory. Sitting directly on top of these open pages is a tiny, hyper-realistic figurine of the scientist sitting at a proportionally tiny wooden desk, working on the very notes beneath him. 

Surroundings: The environment is cluttered with giant-scale period-accurate objects that relate to the scientist's work. This includes a newspaper from the era acting as a backdrop, a giant coffee mug leaving stains, and massive scientific tools relevant to the theory (such as compasses, lenses, or pocket watches) scattered like terrain. 

Perspective: Slightly angled 45-degree macro shot looking down at the notebook. Texture: Wood grain, scratched metal, paper texture, dust particles. Lighting: Warm, late-night library lamp lighting creating a spotlight on the tiny scientist and deep shadows behind the giant props. 

Output: one image, 4:5 aspect ratio, photorealistic historical macro photography. </instructions>
```

### 233. 高中角色时尚搭配提示

**作者**: [シュナプーン](https://x.com/schnapoon/status/2003645877207089179)  **日期**: 2025-12-24  **语言**: ja

> 这是一个为 Nano Banana Pro 设计的详细日式提示模板，它能将参考角色的服装重新排列成三种不同的风格——辣妹（Gal）、优等生（Honor Student）和宅男（Otaku）——同时保持原始颜色和日本高中背景的语境。这对于快速生成背景角色的变体非常有用。

![高中角色时尚搭配提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1766936078607_7noks8_G85gnYRagAMfkX3.jpg)
![高中角色时尚搭配提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1766936079337_8hw40x_G85gpGwagAMFawV.jpg)

```
# 設定
[服装の種類] = {argument name="服装の種類" default="女子高生"}
[世界観] = {argument name="世界観" default="現代日本"}

# 生成の絶対ルール
- 指定された [世界観] に存在しないアイテムは絶対に描写しないこと。
- 「ギャル」「優等生」「オタク」の特徴は、その世界観に馴染むアイテムや着こなしで表現すること。
- 横長のアスペクト比（16:9）で、白背景に以下の4人のキャラクターを左から順に横一列に等間隔に配置してください。全員全身を描写し、足元には自然な影をつけてください。

# キャラクター構成（左から右へ）

1. **【ノーマル（参照元）】**
- 着こなし：[服装の種類] の標準的で正統派なデザイン。
- 特徴：自然な笑顔、主人公的な佇まい。

2. **【ギャル風アレンジ（華美と開放）】**
- 概念：派手好き、露出、流行の最先端、自信。
- 服装変形：[服装の種類] の**色はそのまま**。[世界観] の許す範囲で丈を短く、胸元を開ける。肩を出したり、裾をまくるなど大胆に着崩す。
- 装飾：その世界で手に入る「派手なアクセサリー」（宝石、金細工、髪飾り）を多用。
- ポーズ：開放的で自信に満ちたポーズ。

3. **【優等生風アレンジ（規律と格式）】**
- 概念：規則遵守、保守的、知性、清潔感。
- 服装変形：[服装の種類] の**色はそのまま**。[世界観] における「正装」に近い着こなし。肌の露出を抑え、ボタンや紐を完璧に結ぶ。極めて厳格に着る。襟元はきっちり詰め、乱れがない。露出は最小限。
- 装飾：[世界観] に合わせた「知的なアイテム」（書物、巻物、眼鏡、モノクル、記章）。
- ポーズ：背筋を伸ばし、凛とした表情。

4. **【オタク風アレンジ（収集癖と没頭）】**
- 概念：マニアックな趣味、収集癖、実用性重視または無頓着。
- 服装変形：[服装の種類] の**色はそのまま**。[世界観] における「野暮ったい」着こなし。機能性を求めた過剰な重ね着や、服装の汚れ。
- 装飾：[世界観] の「趣味のアイテム」を大量装備（大量のお守り、護符、魔法薬の瓶、収集した素材が入った大きな鞄）。「推し」の概念を、その世界の偶像やシンボルへの執着として表現。
- ポーズ：猫背気味、何かの観察や収集物に夢中になっている様子。眼鏡やゴーグル。

# 画像仕様
- 背景：白背景
- 画風：高品質なアニメスタイル
```

**Related**: [[综合艺术]]、[[日系动漫]]、[[综合动漫]]

### 235. 圣诞天使设计课程吸睛提示（YAML 结构）

**作者**: [いにしえ@AI Creator｜Will Oldgram](https://x.com/old_pgmrs_will/status/2003500005739593872)  **日期**: 2025-12-23  **语言**: en

> 一个高度结构化的、基于 YAML 的提示，用于让 Nano Banana Pro 生成圣诞主题的缩略图或“吸睛”图片。它定义了一个多层构图，包括一个豪华的圣诞室内背景、一个身着圣诞老人服装的 2D 赛璐珞风格动漫天使角色，以及用于“圣诞设计课程”广告的精致排版元素。

![圣诞天使设计课程吸睛提示（YAML 结构）](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1766673374672_2arpl0_G83cJBSbEAAc4fG.jpg)

```
metadata:
title: "Nano Banana Pro Design Course Eyecatch - Christmas Angel Ver."
model_context: "Seasonal Christmas Advertisement mixed with Cute Anime aesthetics"

image_structure:
composition_type: "Full Background + Right Character + Left Decorated Text"
visual_flow: "Left Text (Seasonal Benefit) -> Right Character (AI Generation Result)"

layers:
layer_background_full:
shape: "Covers the entire screen."
content: "Luxurious Christmas interior scene."
details:
elements: "Decorated Christmas trees with glowing lights, piles of wrapped presents, warm fireplace glow, bokeh lights in the background."
atmosphere: "Warm, magical, festive, with soft falling snow or glitter effect."
focus: "Shallow depth of field, blurring the background elements to make the foreground pop."

layer_visual_right:
shape: "Occupies the right half of the screen."
content: "Japanese Kawaii Anime Angel character in Christmas outfit."
style: "2D Cel-shaded anime art, high detail, warm and vibrant colors."
details:
subject: "A cute anime girl with large feathered angel wings."
appearance:
hair: "Silver or platinum blonde hair."
eyes: "Large, sparkling red or green eyes."
clothing: "A festive Santa Claus style dress with fur trim, ribbons, and bells. A small halo or Santa hat on her head."
pose: "Smiling warmly, making a presenting gesture towards the text on the left."
vfx: "Glowing particles and soft light around her wings and halo."

layer_typography_left:
location: "Left-aligned, positioned in the middle-left area."
container: "Elaborate, decorative golden frame or scroll border (Christmas ornament style) around the main text."
elements:
- type: "Header/Hook"
text: "{argument name="ヘッダーテキスト" default="AIで彩る、最高の冬。"}"
style: "Small gold or white text above the main title."

- type: "Main Title"
text: "{argument name="メインタイトル" default="クリスマス\nデザイン講座"}"
style: "Large, ornate, gold or red gradient font with white outline and shadow. Highly decorative."

- type: "Sub-Title/Benefit"
text: "{argument name="サブタイトル" default="Nano Banana Proで\n季節の素材も自由自在！"}"
style: "Smaller white or gold text below the main title."

- type: "Bottom Tagline"
text: "{argument name="ボトムタグライン" default="初心者でもプロ級の輝き"}"
style: "Small text at the bottom, maybe on a ribbon banner element."

style_and_tone:
art_style: "Festive Anime Illustration with Luxurious Background"
color_palette:
primary: "Red, Green, Gold"
secondary: "White (Snow/Wings), Warm light colors"
quality_tags:
- "High resolution"
- "Anime key visual"
- "Detailed background"
- "Atmospheric lighting"
- "Festive"
```

### 236. 逼真的比基尼照片，带严格身份锁定

**作者**: [Retvi](https://x.com/retvikurmi/status/2003482674577789372)  **日期**: 2025-12-23  **语言**: en

> 一个高度技术化、结构化的提示，用于生成一张超现实图像，同时保持与上传的参考图像（1.0 逼真度）完全一致的面部、身体和皮肤纹理。主体身穿浅绿色挂脖比基尼上衣和透明波点纱笼，置身于奢华明亮的室内，窗外可见自然日光和热带植物。

![逼真的比基尼照片，带严格身份锁定](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1766673226836_iet98f_G83M36RagAEhMV3.jpg)

```
[MODEL]
version = photorealistic_v6
quality = ultra
resolution = 8k
aspect_ratio = 3:4
style = cinematic_realism

[REFERENCE_IMAGE]
use_reference = true
face_fidelity = 1.0
body_fidelity = 1.0
instruction = Maintain exact same face, facial features, skin texture, body proportions, and figure as the uploaded image with zero deviation. No beautification, no morphing, no AI face changes.

[SUBJECT]
gender = female
age = same_as_reference
identity = exact_same_person_from_reference
expression = calm, confident, elegant
gaze = looking slightly toward camera
pose = elegant standing pose, relaxed posture

[FACE]
face_shape = unchanged
eyes = unchanged
nose = unchanged
lips = unchanged
skin_texture = realistic, natural
skin_tone = exact_same_as_reference

[HAIR]
style = exact_same_hairstyle_as_reference
length = unchanged
parting = unchanged
texture = natural, realistic

[OUTFIT]
top = light green halter-neck bikini top
top_details = crisscross straps, fitted, elegant
bottom = sheer light green sarong
sarong_details = polka-dot texture, semi-transparent, tied at the hip
fit = flattering, natural drape
no_clothing_change_on_body_shape = true

[BODY]
figure = exact_same_as_reference
proportions = unchanged
no_slimming = true
no_enhancement = true

[ENVIRONMENT]
location = luxurious bright interior
windows = large floor-to-ceiling windows
outside_view = lush tropical foliage, greenery, palm leaves
interior_style = modern luxury, clean, airy
floor = polished or marble
ambience = tropical, serene, high-end

[LIGHTING]
type = natural daylight
source = window light
quality = soft, diffused
shadows = gentle, realistic
skin_highlights = natural

[CAMERA]
shot_type = captivating mid-to-full body shot
angle = eye-level
lens = 50mm DSLR
depth_of_field = shallow
focus = sharp on face and body

[RENDERING_RULES]
photorealistic = true
no_cartoon = true
no_illustration = true
no_anime = true
no_artifacts = true
no_extra_limbs = true
no_distortion = true
no_text = true
no_watermark = true
```

### 243. 波西塔诺 2x2 网格网红照片拍摄提示

**作者**: [Ditherly - Creative AI Hub](https://x.com/ditherly_art/status/2003291973176684919)  **日期**: 2025-12-23  **语言**: en

> 一个详细的 JSON 提示，用于生成一张 2x2 多面板网格照片，其中包含一位网红在意大利波西塔诺私人露台上的逼真参考图像，重点是温暖的黄金时段复古美学和特定的旅行主题姿势。

### 244. 高角度生日晚餐 POV 照片

**作者**: [Dan Reed](https://x.com/daaaaanc/status/2003188699438207394)  **日期**: 2025-12-22  **语言**: en

> 一个 Gemini Nano Banana Pro 提示，用于生成一张时尚生日晚宴的高角度 POV 照片。照片聚焦于拍摄对象迷人的服装（白色缎面或银色亮片）、“光彩照人”的妆容，以及生日蛋糕上摇曳烛光提供的神奇金色灯光，背景则由霓虹灯牌框定。

![高角度生日晚餐 POV 照片](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1766667262403_4tunpf_G8zBgPcXYAAfIiS.jpg)

```
(Vertical 4:5 aspect ratio). A stunning, high-angle "POV" photograph taken at a trendy birthday dinner. The camera looks down slightly at the subject (friend's perspective).

Subject & Outfit: A beautiful young woman sits at the table, looking up directly at the camera with a radiant, magnetic smile and sparkling eyes.
*   Outfit: She wears a glamorous **{argument name="outfit type" default="White Satin Corset Top"}** or a **{argument name="outfit type 2" default="Silver Sequin Dress"}** with thin straps. The light-colored fabric illuminates her skin and adds a "celebratory goddess" vibe.
*   Hair & Makeup: Her hair is styled in voluminous blowout waves. Her makeup is "glowy and dewy", reflecting the warm light.

Action: She is caught in a candid moment of joy. One hand is playfully touching her hair or resting near her collarbone. In front of her on the table is the birthday cake with flickering candles.

Background (Depth): Behind her (seen from above) is the dark tropical plant wall with the neon sign "IT'S MY BIRTHDAY". Because of the high angle, the neon sign frames her head beautifully without being blocked.

Lighting (Golden Glow): The lighting is magical. The warm golden light from the cake candles illuminates her face from below, mixing with the soft ambient restaurant light. Her eyes catch the reflection of the candle flames (catchlights), making them look bright and alive. The background neon casts a soft purple/pink rim light on her hair.
```

### 249. 配对时尚生成提示

**作者**: [シュナプーン](https://x.com/schnapoon/status/2002993050189209830)  **日期**: 2025-12-22  **语言**: ja

> 这是一个为 Nano Banana Pro 设计的提示词，旨在生成一个男性角色的服装，该服装与参考图片中女性角色的服装形成“一对”或互补。它包含一个设置部分，用于自定义女性服装类型、发色、眼睛颜色和主题颜色，并提供转换规则（例如，水手服转换为学兰/西装外套），以确保男性服装在保持配对主题的同时符合社会规范。

![配对时尚生成提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1766667412614_8qstwp_G8wO2YkbkAAiLQk.jpg)
![配对时尚生成提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1766667413740_ht8obt_G8wO2-2bcAAEC_z.jpg)

```
【設定セクション】
[女性の服装名]: {argument name="女性の服装名" default="セーラー服"}
[髪の色]: {argument name="髪の色" default="黒髪"}
[瞳の色]: {argument name="瞳の色" default="青色の瞳"}
[テーマカラー]: {argument name="テーマカラー" default="水色と白"}
[スタイルの雰囲気]: 繊細なアニメ塗り、清潔感、白い背景のキャラクター立ち絵

【生成プロンプト本文】
最高品質のアニメーションイラスト。
1人の少年（男性キャラクター）。全身図。
髪の色は[髪の色]、目の色は[瞳の色]です。

《服装の指示》
彼は、[女性の服装名]と社会通念上「対（つい）」となる男性用の服装を着用しています。
・重要：[女性の服装名]が女性特有のデザイン（例：セーラー服、ドレス、振袖）である場合、女性服のデザインをそのまま適用せず、それに対応する男性の正装や制服に変換してください。
（変換例：セーラー服なら「学ラン」または「ブレザー」、振袖なら「紋付袴」、ドレスなら「タキシード」）
・服装の配色は[テーマカラー]を取り入れ、ペア感を演出してください。

絵のスタイルは、添付画像のような繊細なラインと鮮やかな色彩を持つ現代的なアニメ調で、背景はシンプルな白です。
```

### 251. 2x2 网格照片生成，带身份锁定

**作者**: [Ditherly - Creative AI Hub](https://x.com/ditherly_art/status/2002944687007809825)  **日期**: 2025-12-22  **语言**: en

> 一个高度结构化的 JSON 提示，用于 Nano Banana Pro 创建一个 2x2 多面板图像网格，其中包含同一主体在黄金时段田野场景中的图像。该提示强制执行严格的身份锁定，确保面部、头发和服装在所有四个画面中保持一致，同时为每个面板改变姿势、拍摄类型和表情。

![2x2 网格照片生成，带身份锁定](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1766667266733_3xtsk2_G8tGssiWcAEkmZ2.jpg)

```
{
  "generation_request": {
    "meta_data": {
      "tool": "NanoBananaPro",
      "task_type": "photorealistic_multi_panel_grid",
      "version": "v1.0",
      "priority": "high"
    },
    "output_settings": {
      "layout": {
        "type": "2x2_grid",
        "border": "thin_cream_gutter",
        "frame_consistency_rule": "same_person_same_outfit_same_field"
      },
      "aspect_ratio": "4:5",
      "resolution": "ultra_high_res",
      "render_style": "analog_film_kodak_portra_400"
    },
    "reference_constraints": {
      "character_reference_image": "UPLOAD_REF_IMAGE",
      "use_reference_face_only": true,
      "identity_lock": true,
      "strict_face_match": true,
      "preserve_facial_structure": true,
      "preserve_skin_tone": true,
      "preserve_hair": true,
      "no_face_mixing": true,
      "no_extra_people": true
    },
    "global_prompt": {
      "scene": "Tall grass field during golden hour sunset. Warm lens flares, dust motes dancing in light. A checkered picnic blanket is visible. Dreamy, romantic, soft focus atmosphere.",
      "subject": {
        "type": "young adult woman",
        "identity": "same person as reference image",
        "hair": "loose waves with a silk ribbon tied in a half-up style",
        "makeup": "no-makeup makeup look, sun-kissed freckles, flushed cheeks",
        "outfit": "white linen milkmaid dress with puffy sleeves and corset detail, bare feet",
        "prop": "vintage hardcover book and a green apple"
      },
      "camera": {
        "capture": "analog film",
        "lens_equivalent": "50mm",
        "focus": "soft focus",
        "depth_of_field": "medium"
      }
    },
    "frames": [
      {
        "frame_id": "A",
        "position": "top_left",
        "shot_type": "high_angle_looking_down",
        "pose": "Lying on back on the picnic blanket, holding the book above face to block the sun, hair spread out.",
        "expression": "playful, laughing"
      },
      {
        "frame_id": "B",
        "position": "top_right",
        "shot_type": "seated_profile",
        "pose": "Sitting cross-legged, biting into the green apple, looking toward the sunset horizon.",
        "expression": "peaceful, content"
      },
      {
        "frame_id": "C",
        "position": "bottom_left",
        "shot_type": "waist_up",
        "pose": "Walking through the tall grass, hands brushing the tops of the wheat, looking back at camera.",
        "expression": "inviting, candid"
      },
      {
        "frame_id": "D",
        "position": "bottom_right",
        "shot_type": "macro_detail",
        "pose": "Close up on hands holding the open book, face slightly out of focus in background.",
        "expression": "focused reading"
      }
    ]
  }
}
```

### 253. 2x2 网格复古餐厅照片拍摄提示

**作者**: [Ditherly - Creative AI Hub](https://x.com/ditherly_art/status/2002804053030621517)  **日期**: 2025-12-21  **语言**: en

> 一个结构化提示，用于生成一个 2x2 网格的逼真图像，其中包含同一个角色（基于参考图像），置身于复古的 50 年代美式餐厅场景中。该提示指定了“闪光流行色”风格、详细的主体外观（扎着辫子、穿着滚边 T 恤、拿着奶昔道具），以及四种不同的姿势/表情（大口吸吮、诱惑地咬樱桃、无聊地等待、傻笑）。

![2x2 网格复古餐厅照片拍摄提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1766489472351_zlcmwr_G8tjp8TXsAAc6nB.jpg)

```
{
    "generation_request": {
      "meta_data": { "tool": "NanoBananaPro", "task_type": "photorealistic_multi_panel_grid", "version": "v1.0" },
      "output_settings": { "layout": { "type": "2x2_grid", "border": "thin_white_gutter", "frame_consistency_rule": "same_person_same_outfit" }, "aspect_ratio": "4:5", "resolution": "ultra_high_res", "render_style": "flash_pop_color" },
      "reference_constraints": { "character_reference_image": "{argument name="character reference image" default="UPLOAD_REF_IMAGE"}", "use_reference_face_only": true, "identity_lock": true, "strict_face_match": true },
      "global_prompt": {
        "scene": "American Diner, retro 50s style. Red leather booths, checkerboard floor, neon sign outside window.",
        "subject": {
          "type": "influencer",
          "identity": "same person as reference image",
          "hair": "high pigtails with ribbons",
          "makeup": "winged liner, freckles",
          "outfit": "cropped ringer tee, denim shorts, knee high socks, converse",
          "prop": "strawberry milkshake with two straws and cherry"
        },
        "camera": { "capture": "retro flash", "lens_equivalent": "35mm", "focus": "subject", "depth_of_field": "sharp" }
      },
      "frames": [
        { "frame_id": "A", "position": "top_left", "shot_type": "sipping_milkshake", "pose": "Sipping milkshake aggressively, looking up at camera under lashes.", "expression": "playful, innocent" },
        { "frame_id": "B", "position": "top_right", "shot_type": "cherry_bite", "pose": "Holding the cherry by the stem near mouth.", "expression": "seductive, fun" },
        { "frame_id": "C", "position": "bottom_left", "shot_type": "booth_knees", "pose": "Kneeling on the booth seat, looking out the window.", "expression": "bored, waiting" },
        { "frame_id": "D", "position": "bottom_right", "shot_type": "messy_face", "pose": "Swipe of whipped cream on nose, laughing.", "expression": "goofy" }
      ]
    }
  }
```

### 254. 2x2 网格意大利餐馆快闪拍摄提示

**作者**: [Ditherly - Creative AI Hub](https://x.com/ditherly_art/status/2002802846232612936)  **日期**: 2025-12-21  **语言**: en

> 一个结构化的提示词，用于生成一个 2x2 的逼真图像网格，其中包含同一个角色（基于参考图像），置身于光线昏暗的意大利小餐馆中。该提示词指定了“直射闪光灯高对比度颗粒感”的风格，详细描述了人物的外观（盘发、黑色露肩上衣、金色大耳环），以及四个与用餐相关的不同姿势/表情（卷意面、开怀大笑饮酒、被闪光灯晃到、慵懒地斜倚）。

![2x2 网格意大利餐馆快闪拍摄提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1766489473469_wwh6r4_G8tikmtWkAAA0Lp.jpg)

```
{
  "generation_request": {
    "meta_data": { "tool": "NanoBananaPro", "task_type": "photorealistic_multi_panel_grid", "version": "v1.0" },
    "output_settings": {
      "layout": { "type": "2x2_grid", "border": "thin_black_gutter", "frame_consistency_rule": "same_person_same_outfit_same_restaurant" },
      "aspect_ratio": "4:5", "resolution": "ultra_high_res", "render_style": "direct_flash_high_contrast_grainy"
    },
    "reference_constraints": {
      "character_reference_image": "{argument name="character reference image" default="UPLOAD_REF_IMAGE"}", "use_reference_face_only": true, "identity_lock": true, "strict_face_match": true
    },
    "global_prompt": {
      "scene": "Dimly lit Italian trattoria at night. White tablecloths. Wine glasses. Plate of pasta. Background is dark and blurry.",
      "subject": {
        "type": "influencer",
        "identity": "same person as reference image",
        "hair": "updo with claw clip, messy face-framing pieces",
        "makeup": "glowy skin, brushed up brows, bitten lip look",
        "outfit": "black off-the-shoulder top (tight), gold hoop earrings, layered necklaces",
        "prop": "fork with pasta or glass of red wine"
      },
      "camera": { "capture": "hard flash", "lens_equivalent": "28mm", "focus": "subject", "depth_of_field": "sharp foreground" }
    },
    "frames": [
      { "frame_id": "A", "position": "top_left", "shot_type": "twirling_pasta", "pose": "Looking down at the pasta, twirling a massive amount on a fork. Flash reflecting off the sauce.", "expression": "focused, hungry" },
      { "frame_id": "B", "position": "top_right", "shot_type": "wine_laugh", "pose": "Holding wine glass by the stem, head thrown back laughing at someone across the table. Hand covering mouth slightly.", "expression": "candid joy" },
      { "frame_id": "C", "position": "bottom_left", "shot_type": "flash_blinded", "pose": "Holding hand up to block the flash, eyes squinting, looking directly at lens.", "expression": "playful annoyance" },
      { "frame_id": "D", "position": "bottom_right", "shot_type": "messy_table", "pose": "Leaning elbows on the table, chin in hands, looking seductive/tired. Table is messy with empty plates.", "expression": "sultry" }
    ]
  }
}
```

> 一个高度具体的 JSON 提示，描述了一位具有 coquette/兔女郎风格的年轻女性，她坐在台球桌的边缘。提示详细描述了她的外貌（金色的金发，红润的脸颊）、着装（淡粉色天鹅绒紧身胸衣，白色渔网袜，兔耳朵）、姿势以及环境（浅橡木台球桌，现代枝形吊灯，柔和的室内日光）。

{
  "detailed_prompt": {
    "subject": {
      "skin": "{argument name="skin tone" default="Fair with warm peach undertones, smooth texture, soft sheen on shoulders"}",

      "eyes": "{argument name="eye color" default="Blue-grey, almond shape, direct confident gaze"}",

    },

      "seating": "Perched on light oak wooden rail of pool table",

      "right_hand_placement": "Arm extended straight down, palm pressed flat onto black felt surface, fingers splayed",
      "left_hand_placement": "Arm bent close to body, hand resting gently on upper thigh of crossed leg"
    },
    "attire": {
      "headwear": "Large white satin bunny ears on headband",

### 256. 每周穿搭设计灵感

**作者**: [Dr.D](https://x.com/Dyorzheng/status/2002645669958324661)  **日期**: 2025-12-21  **语言**: zh

> 这是一个为 Nano Banana Pro 设计的提示，用于生成一张 16:9 的横向图像。图像中展示了同一位女性角色的七个全身像，每个形象代表一周中的一天，并根据用户定义的主题或场景，拥有独特的服装、姿势和表情。AI 被指示自由设计服装、姿势和氛围，但要求这七个人物明显是同一个人。

![每周穿搭设计灵感](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1766489528357_be6alk_G8rTTETW4AAK3QI.jpg)
![每周穿搭设计灵感](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1766489528350_gnyq08_G8rTdm6WIAA1Ubd.jpg)
![每周穿搭设计灵感](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1766489528888_k7w5l8_G8rTfVTXwAAFyqA.jpg)
![每周穿搭设计灵感](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1766489529879_vlg2pg_G8rTh5BWUAAdU4q.jpg)

```
严格参考图中人物
画面中出现同一个女性的7个形象，对应一周的七天
明确为同一个人，
但允许她们拥有符合主题或者场景的不同的姿态、表情、动作与穿着。
主题 / 场景：
[{argument name="主题 / 场景" default=""}]
请 AI 根据该主题自由设计：
服装搭配
姿态与动作
表情与气质
整体氛围与风格
不需要统一风格，
不需要刻意对齐姿势，
不需要明确规定情绪或动作。
画面要求：
横向构图（16:9）
全身呈现
多个同一人物并排出现
整体自然、真实、有变化
背景中可以加一些符合场景和主题的手账图案
上方有个符合主题的中文标题
主体名字叫[{argument name="主体名字" default=""}]，其余的标题内容你自己设计
不要分析，直接出图
```

**作者**: [Lex](https://x.com/lexx_aura/status/2002408866911301756)  **日期**: 2025-12-20  **语言**: en

> 一个用于 Nano Banana Pro 的 JSON 提示词，旨在生成一张具有 2000 年代数码相机美学、类似于狗仔队偷拍快照的图像。图像中，一位深色波浪发年轻女子回头望向肩后，身穿露背挂脖上衣。关键元素包括强烈的直射闪光灯照明、浓重的阴影以及复古数码传感器特有的轻微颗粒感。

      "expression": "Confident, subtle smile, alluring eye contact",

    },
    "outfit": {
      "garment": "Black halter-neck top or dress",
      "fit": "Form-fitting, sleeveless",
      "cut": "Completely backless, low side cut revealing side profile"
    },
    "pose": {
      "orientation": "Rear/side view, torso twisted towards camera",
      "arms": "Right arm raised, elbow bent upwards, hand grasping hair at the crown",
      "hands": "Fingers visible in hair, wearing multiple gold rings",
      "nails": "Black polish"
    },
    "environment": {
      "setting": "Indoor bedroom or closet space",
      "background": "White wardrobe doors with silver knobs (right), beige walls, white doorframe (left)",
      "depth": "Shallow depth of field but background features are distinguishable"
    },
    "technical_style": {

      "lighting": "Hard direct flash, strong shadows cast on the wall behind subject",

### 260. 90 年代跳跳球玩具自拍，低角度拍摄

**作者**: [Sienna](https://x.com/siennalovesai/status/2002385437953044903)  **日期**: 2025-12-20  **语言**: en

> 一个结构化的提示，用于生成一张超逼真的“原始自拍”，这张自拍是用模拟智能手机摄像头从地板的低角度拍摄的，画面中一位运动型女性身处 90 年代跳跳球玩具主题的卧室中，强调活力和怀旧感。

![90 年代跳跳球玩具自拍，低角度拍摄](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1766385947060_7bu5bi_G8nm7-aWYAAavfT.jpg)
![90 年代跳跳球玩具自拍，低角度拍摄](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1766385947289_s5b40s_G8nm7-bXEAA7F8g.jpg)

```
{
  "meta": {
    "aspect_ratio": "9:16",
    "quality": "ultra_photorealistic",
    "resolution": "8k",
    "camera": "smartphone front camera",
    "lens": "24mm",
    "style": "raw selfie, high realism, no over-smoothing"
  },
  "scene": {
    "location": "90s Skip-It toy themed bedroom",
    "setting": "Skip-It toys in various colors on floor, jump rope and hula hoop hanging, 90s active toy posters, counter device for skips, play area rug",
    "time": "afternoon",
    "atmosphere": "active play nostalgia, energetic confidence"
  },
  "lighting": {
    "type": "bright natural",
    "source": "window sunlight",
    "effect": "playful highlights"
  },
  "camera_perspective": {
    "pov": "WE ARE THE CAMERA",
    "angle": "low from floor",
    "distance": "arm-length extended",
    "framing": "full body to head"
  },
  "subject": {
    "gender": "female",
    "age": "early 20s (clearly adult)",
    "ethnicity": "{argument name="ethnicity" default="Australian"}",
    "body": {
      "type": "athletic"
    },
    "skin": {
      "tone": "fair tan"
    },
    "hair": {
      "color": "blonde",
      "style": "ponytail"
    },
    "face": {
      "expression": "playful grin"
    },
    "outfit": {
      "top": {
        "type": "tank top",
        "color": "white"
      },
      "bottom": {
        "type": "shorts"
      }
    }
  },
  "details": [
    "Skip-It on floor",
    "jump rope hanging",
    "active energy",
    "no camera or phone artifacts visible"
  ]
}
```

### 261. 罗纳尔多体育场自拍身份保留提示

**作者**: [Zara](https://x.com/ZaraIrahh/status/2002320492548722766)  **日期**: 2025-12-20  **语言**: en

> 这是一个为 Nano Banana Pro 设计的复杂 JSON 提示词，旨在生成一张与克里斯蒂亚诺·罗纳尔多 (Cristiano Ronaldo) 在足球场上的超逼真自拍照。该提示词要求 100% 保留上传的女性参考面部特征，并将其置于罗纳尔多旁边。它详细描述了拍摄对象的表情、服装（黄色球衣、黑色上衣）以及环境（欢呼的人群、体育场泛光灯），风格为抓拍式高分辨率。

![罗纳尔多体育场自拍身份保留提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1766385918382_dewiyh_G8mr27TakAAsqBb.jpg)

```
{
  "image_prompt": {
    "reference": {
      "face_identity": "uploaded reference image",
      "identity_lock": true,
      "face_preservation": "100% identical facial structure, proportions, skin texture, eye shape, lips, nose, brows, moles, and natural expression"
    },

    "subjects": [
      {
        "type": "young woman",
        "role": "foreground subject",
        "expression": "soft confident smile",
        "gaze": "looking directly at the camera",
        "pose": {
          "position": "standing very close to the male subject",
          "interaction": "leaning slightly toward him in a casual selfie pose"
        },
        "hair": {
          "color": "dark brown",
          "style": "sleek high ponytail"
        },
        "makeup": {
          "style": "natural glam",
          "details": [
            "even glowing skin",
            "subtle contour",
            "soft blush",
            "defined brows",
            "natural pink lips"
          ]
        },
        "outfit": {
          "clothing": "black fitted short-sleeve top",
          "style": "sporty casual"
        }
      },
      {
        "type": "Cristiano Ronaldo",
        "role": "secondary subject",
        "expression": "relaxed smile",
        "gaze": "looking at the camera",
        "hair": {
          "color": "dark brown",
          "style": "short, neatly styled"
        },
        "outfit": {
          "clothing": "bright yellow football jersey",
          "details": [
            "team logo visible",
            "athletic fit"
          ]
        }
      }
    ],

    "environment": {
      "location": "football stadium",
      "background_elements": [
        "large cheering crowd",
        "stadium seating filled with fans",
        "players and staff visible in the distance",
        "night sky with stadium floodlights"
      ]
    },

    "lighting": {
      "type": "stadium lighting",
      "characteristics": [
        "bright overhead lights",
        "even illumination on faces",
        "slight highlights on skin",
        "realistic night-time contrast"
      ]
    },

    "photography_style": {
      "style": "real-life selfie photography",
      "camera_look": "smartphone camera",
      "depth_of_field": "moderate depth of field with slightly blurred crowd",
      "mood": "excited, celebratory, candid"
    },

    "render_quality": {
      "realism": "ultra-photorealistic",
      "detail_level": "high",
      "Aspect Ratio": "4:5",
      "skin_texture": "natural and realistic",
      "resolution": "high resolution",
      "color_grading": "true-to-life colors with stadium vibrancy"
    }
  }
}
```

### 262. 90 年代追星女孩自拍提示词（韩国主题）

**作者**: [Sienna](https://x.com/siennalovesai/status/2002207326145507671)  **日期**: 2025-12-20  **语言**: en

> 一个为 Nano Banana Pro 3.0 设计的详细 JSON 提示，用于生成一张具有 90 年代美学风格的超逼真原始自拍照。场景是一个贴满了男团海报的追星女孩卧室。主体是一位身材苗条、沙漏型身材的年轻韩国女性，身穿紧身露脐短上衣和格子迷你裙，摆姿势坐在床上，手里拿着一个 CD 盒。

![90 年代追星女孩自拍提示词（韩国主题）](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1766385911663_tvm3d8_G8i7y5sXsAEXPOj.jpg)

```
{
  "meta": {
    "aspect_ratio": "9:16",
    "quality": "ultra_photorealistic",
    "resolution": "8k",
    "camera": "smartphone front camera",
    "lens": "24mm",
    "style": "raw selfie, high realism, no over-smoothing"
  },
  "scene": {
    "location": "90s boy band fangirl bedroom",
    "setting": "walls covered in {argument name="band posters" default="NSYNC, Backstreet Boys, 98 Degrees"} posters, CD tower with jewel cases, butterfly chair, heart-shaped pillows, magazine cutouts pinned up, cassette tapes",
    "time": "night",
    "atmosphere": "90s teen crush nostalgia, playful confidence"
  },
  "lighting": {
    "type": "soft lamp",
    "source": "bedside heart lamp + TV glow",
    "effect": "warm pinkish highlights"
  },
  "camera_perspective": {
    "pov": "WE ARE THE CAMERA",
    "angle": "slightly low angle from bed",
    "distance": "arm-length extended",
    "framing": "full body to head, posters visible",
    "phone_visibility": "not visible"
  },
  "subject": {
    "gender": "female",
    "age": "early 20s (clearly adult)",
    "ethnicity": "Korean",
    "body": {
      "type": "slim hourglass",
      "waist": "tiny",
      "hips": "curved",
      "ass": "toned",
      "chest": "full",
      "legs": "long"
    },
    "skin": {
      "tone": "light with warm undertone",
      "detail": "dewy glow",
      "cheeks": "subtle blush"
    },
    "hair": {
      "color": "dark brown with chunky highlights",
      "length": "long",
      "style": "90s layered cut with butterfly clips",
      "behavior": "voluminous"
    },
    "face": {
      "eyes": "dark",
      "expression": "sweet confident smile",
      "brows": "straight",
      "lips": "shiny gloss",
      "vibe": "fangirl allure"
    },
    "pose": {
      "position": "sitting on bed with posters behind",
      "hips": "shifted",
      "torso": "upright",
      "legs": "tucked",
      "arms": {
        "phone_hand": "held out front",
        "free_hand": "holding CD case"
      }
    },
    "outfit": {
      "top": {
        "type": "baby tee with boy band logo",
        "color": "white",
        "fit": "tight cropped"
      },
      "bottom": {
        "type": "pleated mini skirt",

      }
    }

### 263. 菲律宾漫画迷在收藏室自拍

**作者**: [Sienna](https://x.com/siennalovesai/status/2002055179353694250)  **日期**: 2025-12-19  **语言**: en

> 为 Gemini Nano Banana Pro 3.0 生成的超逼真图像提示，模拟一位娇小丰满的菲律宾女性在复古漫画收藏家的卧室里拍摄的原始自拍照。提示详细描述了环境（摆满漫画书的书架、海报）、拍摄对象的服装（超级英雄图案 T 恤、牛仔短裤）和灯光（暖色阅读灯），旨在营造一种“极客怀旧”和“自信魅力”的美学。

![菲律宾漫画迷在收藏室自拍](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1766238170940_hcq0pf_G8i6kIRXwAUPi2j.jpg)

{

    "resolution": "8k",

    "lens": "24mm",
    "style": "raw selfie, high realism, no over-smoothing"
  },
  "scene": {
    "location": "vintage comic book collector bedroom",
    "setting": "shelves of bagged and boarded comics, classic Marvel and DC posters, action figures in boxes, reading lamp over chair, longboxes under bed, retro comic rug",
    "time": "evening",
    "atmosphere": "geek nostalgia, confident allure"
  },

    "effect": "dramatic shadows and highlights"
  },

    "pov": "WE ARE THE CAMERA",
    "angle": "slightly low angle from chair level",
    "distance": "arm-length extended",
    "framing": "full body to head, comics visible",
    "phone_visibility": "not visible"
  },
  "subject": {
    "gender": "female",

    "ethnicity": "Filipina",
    "body": {
      "type": "petite curvy",

      "hips": "full",

    },

    },

### 264. 逼真的 MacBook 屏幕 POV 自拍提示词

**作者**: [Zaylee](https://x.com/zayleeai/status/2001943686897189281)  **日期**: 2025-12-19  **语言**: en

> 一个为 Gemini Nano Banana Pro 设计的复杂 JSON 提示词，用于图像到图像的生成，重点在于创建一个超现实的 POV 视角，向下俯视 MacBook 屏幕。屏幕上显示的是 Photo Booth 的实时预览，主体（其身份严格保留自输入照片）身处昏暗的卧室中，背景播放着 Spotify。该提示词强调真实感细节，如 RGB 像素网格、灰尘和自然噪点，模拟的是对屏幕拍摄的照片，而非屏幕截图。

![逼真的 MacBook 屏幕 POV 自拍提示词](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1766238131733_pupigj_G8hVJz0WYAAPNF8.jpg)
![逼真的 MacBook 屏幕 POV 自拍提示词](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1766238132202_vjl9h1_G8hVJz2XgAAPuVH.jpg)

```
{
  "image_settings": {
    "aspect_ratio": "3:4",
    "resolution": {
      "width": 1152,
      "height": 1536
    }
  },

  "prompt": {
    "identity_lock": {
      "reference": "{argument name="reference" default="input_photo"}",
      "preserve": [
        "{argument name="preserve 1" default="face"}",
        "{argument name="preserve 2" default="facial proportions"}",
        "{argument name="preserve 3" default="eye shape"}",
        "{argument name="preserve 4" default="nose"}",
        "{argument name="preserve 5" default="lips"}",
        "{argument name="preserve 6" default="skin tone"}",
        "{argument name="preserve 7" default="skin texture"}",
        "{argument name="preserve 8" default="hairline"}",
        "{argument name="preserve 9" default="overall identity"}"
      ],
      "rules": [
        "{argument name="rule 1" default="no face swap"}",
        "{argument name="rule 2" default="no beautify"}",
        "{argument name="rule 3" default="no smoothing"}",
        "{argument name="rule 4" default="no reshaping"}",
        "{argument name="rule 5" default="no AI look"}"
      ]
    },

    "scene": {
      "camera_angle": "{argument name="camera angle" default="high-angle downward shot, POV"}",
      "composition": "{argument name="composition" default="MacBook screen fills most of the frame, thin strip of physical keyboard visible at the bottom"}",
      "screen_surface": [
        "{argument name="screen surface 1" default="visible RGB pixel grid"}",
        "{argument name="screen surface 2" default="subtle moire effect"}",
        "{argument name="screen surface 3" default="micro dust on glass"}",
        "{argument name="screen surface 4" default="faint fingerprints"}",
        "{argument name="screen surface 5" default="soft ambient reflections"}"
      ]
    },

    "digital_interface": {
      "os": "{argument name="os" default="macOS dark mode"}",
      "background_app": {
        "name": "{argument name="background app name" default="Spotify"}",
        "view": "{argument name="background app view" default="Liked Songs"}",
        "visible_tracks": [
          "{argument name="track 1" default="Blank Space – Taylor Swift"}",
          "{argument name="track 2" default="Shake It Off – Taylor Swift"}",
          "{argument name="track 3" default="Cruel Summer – Taylor Swift"}",
          "{argument name="track 4" default="Love Story – Taylor Swift"}"
        ]
      },
      "foreground_app": {
        "name": "{argument name="foreground app name" default="Photo Booth"}",
        "state": "{argument name="foreground app state" default="live preview window"}",
        "position": "{argument name="foreground app position" default="floating, center-right"}"
      }
    },

    "photo_booth_content": {
      "environment": {
        "room": "{argument name="room" default="dim bedroom"}",
        "background": "{argument name="background" default="off-white wall, rumpled bedding"}",
        "lighting": "{argument name="lighting" default="low-light, nocturnal, cool screen glow mixed with warm skin tones"}"
      },
      "subject": {
        "pose": "{argument name="subject pose" default="lying down, relaxed, candid"}",
        "expression": "{argument name="subject expression" default="natural, slightly relaxed"}",
        "outfit": "{argument name="subject outfit" default="light-colored tank top"}",
        "prop": {
          "item": "{argument name="prop item" default="iPhone 15 Pro"}",
          "hand": "{argument name="prop hand" default="right hand"}"
        }
      }
    },

    "realism_rules": [
      "{argument name="realism rule 1" default="this is a photo of a screen, not a screenshot"}",
      "{argument name="realism rule 2" default="raw smartphone photo look"}",
      "{argument name="realism rule 3" default="natural noise"}",
      "{argument name="realism rule 4" default="imperfect glass"}",
      "{argument name="realism rule 5" default="no studio lighting"}",
      "{argument name="realism rule 6" default="no HD polish"}"
    ]
  },

  "negative_prompt": [
    "{argument name="negative 1" default="screenshot"}",
    "{argument name="negative 2" default="flat UI"}",
    "{argument name="negative 3" default="perfect screen"}",
    "{argument name="negative 4" default="clean glass"}",
    "{argument name="negative 5" default="studio lighting"}",
    "{argument name="negative 6" default="beauty filter"}",
    "{argument name="negative 7" default="cartoon"}",
    "{argument name="negative 8" default="3d render"}",
    "{argument name="negative 9" default="painting"}",
    "{argument name="negative 10" default="watermark"}",
    "{argument name="negative 11" default="blurred face"}"
  ]
}
```

### 265. 全身海滩场景图像生成提示

**作者**: [Lore](https://x.com/l_w_lorenzen/status/2001664335995900418)  **日期**: 2025-12-18  **语言**: en

> 一个详细的 JSON 提示，用于 Nano Banana Pro 生成一张高分辨率、逼真的图像：一名年轻女性身穿绿松石色比基尼，斜倚在一辆复古的绿松石色汽车旁，置身于阳光明媚的海滩上。该提示强调了身份保留和特定的相机/灯光设置。

![全身海滩场景图像生成提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1766237881517_41zwa3_G8dXEsJakAQe-nw.jpg)

```
{

   "prompt_metadata": {     "type": "image_generation",     "quality": "high-resolution",     "detail_level": "very high",     "constraints": {       "identity_preservation": {         "enabled": true,         "description": "100% same face and body details must be preserved"       }     }   },   "subject": {     "category": "human",     "gender": "female",     "age_group": "young adult",     "appearance": {       "face": {         "preserve_original_features": true,         "expression": "calm and confident",         "gaze_direction": "looking directly at the viewer"       },       "body": {         "visibility": "full body",         "description": "beautiful, proportionate, natural anatomy"       },       "hair": {         "color": "{argument name="hair color" default="dark brown"}",         "length": "medium to long",         "texture": "slightly wavy",         "style": "loose and natural"       }     }   },   "wardrobe": {     "primary_outfit": {       "type": "bikini",       "color": "{argument name="bikini color" default="turquoise"}",       "style": "modern beachwear",       "fit": "form-fitting"     }   },   "pose_and_action": {     "stance": "standing",     "body_position": "leaning casually",     "interaction": {       "object": "vintage car",       "description": "leaning in front of the car"     }   },   "props": {     "handheld_item": {       "type": "drink",       "liquid_color": "{argument name="drink color" default="green"}",       "container_style": "transparent cup",       "straw": {         "color": "red"       }     }   },   "environment": {     "setting": "beach",     "weather": "sunny",     "time_of_day": "daytime",     "background_elements": {       "sky": {         "color": "bright blue",         "clouds": "scattered white clouds"       },       "ocean": {         "visibility": "clearly visible",         "color": "blue",         "position": "behind the subject"       },       "sand": {         "description": "light-colored beach sand"       }     }   },   "objects": {     "vehicle": {       "type": "car",       "style": "vintage",       "color": "{argument name="car color" default="turquoise"}",       "condition": "well-maintained",       "position": "behind the subject, used as a prop"     }   },   "lighting_and_color": {     "lighting_type": "natural sunlight",     "illumination": "bright and even",     "shadows": "soft, minimal harsh contrast",     "color_palette": [       "turquoise",       "blue",       "green",       "sand beige"     ]   },   "camera_and_composition": {     "shot_type": "full-body shot",     "camera_angle": "eye-level",     "focus": "sharp focus on subject",     "depth_of_field": "moderate, background slightly softened",     "framing": "subject centered with environment clearly visible"   
}
```

### 266. Y2K 魅力自拍，附带造型变体

**作者**: [yusra.](https://x.com/chatgptpaglu/status/2001610934217777378)  **日期**: 2025-12-18  **语言**: en

> 一个复杂的图像生成提示，用于生成一张年轻女性的高质量自拍。该提示要求使用参考图像来锁定身份，并提供两种截然不同的造型变体：一种是波西米亚华丽风（Boho Glam），搭配叠戴金色首饰；另一种是时尚千禧年风（Sleek Y2K），搭配白色紧身胸衣和极简配饰。所有图像都采用温暖的闪光灯电影摄影风格。

![Y2K 魅力自拍，附带造型变体](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1766936180505_3r0wiq_G8cmiR0W8AA3gcI.jpg)

```
{
  "image_prompt_structure": {
    "meta_settings": {
      "aspect_ratio": "3:4",
      "reference_image_mode": "img2img",
      "reference_strength": "High (Do not change physical features)"
    },
    "subject_core": {
      "demographics": "Young woman",
      "pose": {
        "angle": "Selfie, slightly elevated",
        "head_position": "Slightly tilted",
        "eye_contact": "Directly at camera"
      },
      "expression": {
        "mood": "Confident, sensual",
        "mouth": "Lips pursed in a thin pout (blowing a kiss)"
      },
      "facial_details": {

### 269. 写实级 PVC 人偶产品介绍布局

**作者**: [てんねん](https://x.com/munou_ac/status/2001238094457266531)  **日期**: 2025-12-17  **语言**: ja

> 这是一个为 Nano Banana Pro 设计的综合性提示，旨在根据参考图像为 PVC 人偶生成一个超逼真的产品介绍布局。它包含了人偶设计的详细规格、构图（垂直 3:4 比例，包含主视觉和产品信息区域）、动作（静态姿势）、场景（中性摄影棚环境）、风格（超逼真渲染）、灯光（摄影棚灯光，带有光泽/哑光效果），以及产品名称、制造商、比例、价格、尺寸和材料的精确日文文本元素，包括多个突出不同特征的特写插图面板。

![写实级 PVC 人偶产品介绍布局](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1766936084166_akbdxh_G8XTcGNaAAAmLN5.jpg)
![写实级 PVC 人偶产品介绍布局](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1766936084050_etec6l_G8XTcGRaAAA3_TA.jpg)
![写实级 PVC 人偶产品介绍布局](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1766936084588_wrkfsu_G8XTcGMbUAAghZN.jpg)
![写实级 PVC 人偶产品介绍布局](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1766936086775_0ylrm3_G8XTcGOaoAALjeQ.jpg)

```
product_name: "{ARBITRARY_PRODUCT_NAME}"
manufacturer_name: "{ARBITRARY_MANUFACTURER_NAME}"

subject: >
  The character from reference image A, faithfully preserved in design, proportions,
  facial features, hairstyle, outfit details, and color palette.
  The character is transformed into a highly detailed, photorealistic PVC figure.
  Sculpting style and overall aesthetic are inferred directly from the reference image.
  The figure is presented as a 1/7 scale collectible.

composition: >
  Japanese-language product introduction layout inferred by the model.
  Vertical composition with a 3:4 aspect ratio.
  A large main visual of the full figure.
  A single, clearly defined product information area containing all textual elements.
  Product name logo and manufacturer name logo are each displayed exactly once.
  Multiple inset close-up panels are included.
  Each inset must focus on a different physical area or feature of the figure.
  No two inset panels may depict the same part or the same visual characteristic.
  Inset panels must be visually and conceptually distinct from one another.

action: >
  Static collectible figure pose with no movement.
  Emphasis on sculpt accuracy, proportions, and surface detail.

location: >
  Neutral studio-like environment inferred for product photography.
  Minimal, non-distracting background.

style: >
  Photorealistic product rendering and photography style.
  Artistic tone and mood inferred entirely from the reference image.

camera_lighting: >
  Camera angle and lighting inferred for clear presentation of a collectible figure.
  Realistic studio lighting interacting with PVC surfaces.
  Glossy highlights on hair and clothing.
  Matte finish on skin.
  Sharp focus with natural depth of field.
  Soft shadow beneath the figure as if placed on a flat surface.

colors: >
  Exact color reproduction based on the reference image.
  Background and graphic elements inferred to support readability of Japanese text.

text: >
  商品名：
  「{{product_name}}」
  ※ 商品名は必ず表示し、ロゴとして1箇所のみ表示する。

  メーカー名：
  「{{manufacturer_name}}」
  ※ メーカー名も必ず表示し、ロゴとして1箇所のみ表示する。

  スケール：
  1/7スケールフィギュア

  原型製作：
  {{manufacturer_name}}

  価格：
  フィギュアのスケール、造形密度、塗装表現から推論した
  販売価格を日本円で表示。

  サイズ：
  キャラクターの体型と1/7スケール設定から推論した
  全高をセンチメートル表記で表示。

  材質：
  フィギュアとして妥当な材
```

### 270. AKIRA“滑行刹车场景”复刻提示词

**作者**: [SSSS_CRYPTOMAN](https://x.com/SSSS_CRYPTOMAN/status/2001219867870175289)  **日期**: 2025-12-17  **语言**: en

> 一个针对 Nano Banana Pro 的高度具体、多部分的提示，旨在重现动漫中标志性的“滑行刹车场景”，但不能使用“AKIRA”这个词。它详细描述了构图、主体、动作、视觉效果（烟雾轨迹、霓虹绿能量弧）和艺术风格（20 世纪 80 年代赛博朋克动漫美学）。

![AKIRA“滑行刹车场景”复刻提示词](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1766042133257_8xxu2g_G8XCFwTa4AAeQjX.jpg)
![AKIRA“滑行刹车场景”复刻提示词](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1766042133923_4bgtwn_G8XCFsya4AMdrZS.jpg)
![AKIRA“滑行刹车场景”复刻提示词](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1766042136348_wnfdb8_G8XCFsybQAA148Q.jpg)
![AKIRA“滑行刹车场景”复刻提示词](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1766042133665_q6p1rz_G8XCFs1a4AIHc9R.jpg)

```
(VARIABLE SCENE - EDIT HERE):
Nighttime, expansive {argument name="cityscape" default="Neo-Tokyo"} highway. Futuristic cityscape background with neon lights.
Strong one-point perspective: The road stretches straight from the bottom edge to the vanishing point in the center.

(CRITICAL COMPOSITION):
One-point perspective composition with the subject in the CENTER.
Subject Orientation: The motorcycle is shown in SIDE PROFILE (facing Screen Left).
TILT ANGLE: The motorcycle body is LEANING HEAVILY TOWARDS THE CAMERA (The top of the bike is closer to the viewer than the wheels).
Movement direction: The bike is sliding away from the camera, moving from the foreground deep into the background.
Placement: Bike is perfectly centered in the frame.

(SUBJECT):
A futuristic motorcycle and rider.
Motorcycle:
- Heavy, solid, rounded silhouette
- Minimal exposed mechanics, smooth cowling
- Wide, thick, high-grip tires
- Color scheme harmonized with rider
Rider:
- Face and outfit preserved from reference image
- Stare straight into the camera, glaring with a powerful, piercing gaze.
- Left foot planted firmly on the ground, struggling to support the heavy leaning bike
- Rider's leg is fully extended to brace against the fall

(ACTION & MECHANICS):
High-speed linear slide braking (NOT cornering).
The bike is sliding sideways while traveling backwards into the depth of the scene.
Instability: The bike is on the verge of falling over towards the screen.
Wheels are locked (not rotating).

(VISUAL EFFECTS - SMOKE TRAILS):
Three distinct, straight trails of thick white smoke.
Direction: Smoke stretches from the IMMEDIATE FOREGROUND (bottom of screen) directly to the motorcycle's wheels and rider's foot in the center.
The smoke trails act as leading lines pointing to the subject.
Violent debris and asphalt fragments kicking up.

(ENERGY EFFECTS):
Neon-green lightning energy arcs (1980s anime style) embedded within the white smoke trails.
Green energy flows through the smoke, following the straight lines from foreground to the bike.

(ART STYLE):
Cel-shaded animation, 1980s anime aesthetic (Cyberpunk).
High contrast, bold black shadows, dramatic lighting.
Poster-quality, ultra-high resolution, sharp focus.
```

### 274. 雪山毛皮帽自拍，冬日魅力尽显

**作者**: [Lex](https://x.com/lexx_aura/status/2000468933434880464)  **日期**: 2025-12-15  **语言**: en

> 一张用于生成网红风格图片的提示词，内容为一张高对比度自拍，画面中一位女性戴着超大黑色毛皮帽子，身穿紧身栗色露脐上衣，在严酷明亮的阳光下，对着白雪皑皑的山脉背景呼出清晰可见的水汽，旨在营造一种“辣妹”美学。

![雪山毛皮帽自拍，冬日魅力尽显](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1766936120875_ets373_G8MX4dTXkAAR8F-.jpg)

```
{
  "prompt_details": {
    "subject": {
      "description": "Young woman with a white complexion and long, straight dark brown hair",
      "facial_features": "Sharp eyebrows, brown eyes looking off to the side, defined jawline",
      "makeup": "Light glam makeup, sharp winged black eyeliner, matte dark mauve/brown lipstick, contouring"
    },
    "outfit": {
      "headwear": "Oversized, fluffy {argument name="hat color" default="black"} fur hat (ushanka style)",
      "clothing": "Tight-fitting {argument name="top color" default="maroon/burgundy"} ribbed knit long-sleeve crop top with a low scoop neckline",
      "accessories": "Sparkling silver crystal or diamond tennis choker necklace"
    },
    "pose_and_action": {
      "type": "Selfie shot taken with an extended arm",
      "hand_placement": "Right hand raised, holding the side of the fur hat",
      "action": "Exhaling a cloud of white vapor/breath visually indicating the cold temperature"
    },
    "environment": {
      "location": "High-altitude snowy mountain range (Alps or similar)",

      - "extreme perspective"

  identity:
    ethnicity: "Japanese"

    style: "windy, dressy, Idol costumes that resemble high school girl uniforms"

### 280. 图像标注和赞美评论提示

**作者**: [iX | AI Video Creator](https://x.com/iX00AI/status/1998395439998194144)  **日期**: 2025-12-09  **语言**: ja

> 为 Higgsfield Nano Banana Pro 提供一个详细的提示，该提示能自动分析上传的女性图片，并在图片上直接添加自发、富有表现力且积极的手写日文评论、涂鸦和编辑标记，从而营造出视觉冲击力强烈的个性化剪贴簿美学。

![图像标注和赞美评论提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1765440125413_0yhgam_G7u6DSmagAALwBC.jpg)

```
Add messy red handwritten Japanese comments, expressive doodles, and energetic editorial-style notes directly on top of the image, as if written with a red marker over printed photos. The handwriting should feel spontaneous, unfiltered, emotional, slightly chaotic, and personal—almost like someone’s private photo journal or annotated scrapbook page.

All handwritten text must:
– be in Japanese
– appear hand-drawn, uneven, casual, and overlapping
– be positive in tone

The content of each handwritten note must automatically analyze the uploaded image and praise the woman based on what is visible, such as her outfit, expression, pose, styling, makeup, or mood.
The comments should feel affectionate, admiring, or supportive, and tailored to what stands out in the photo.

Do not repeat generic praise.
Instead, generate unique personal compliments that match the image attributes.

Examples must NOT be shown explicitly in the prompt.
Instead, describe the logic:

“The system should observe the clothing style, face, mood, posture, accessories, or color choices and produce handwritten comments that positively highlight what is visually appealing or admirable about her.”

Also add:
– arrows pointing to notable fashion details
– underlines beneath interesting areas
– circled elements
– crossed-out planning notes like editing marks
– layered cut-and-paste collage scraps (magazine style)
– small torn paper labels
– sticker-like notations
– tape-texture fragments

Overall direction:
Create a visually intense scrapbook-journal composition, filled with affectionate handwriting, red editorial markings, and collage fragments, giving the entire image an emotional and expressive “personal praise commentary” aesthetic.
```

**作者**: [た〜や｜AI副業ワーママ](https://x.com/taya_mama_AI/status/1997836036328816722)  **日期**: 2025-12-08  **语言**: en

> 一个为 Nano Banana Pro 设计的详细提示词，可将上传的图像（真实照片或现有角色）转换为两头身比例的超萌 Q 版角色，将其渲染成一个小型 3D 模型，并放置在一个玻璃雪球中，雪球内有一个微型雪景小镇和圣诞灯光散景背景。

Use the uploaded image as the only character reference.
CONDITION

Then render that chibi as a small cute 3D figure.
Keep the character’s key identity (face shape, hairstyle, hair color, outfit colors, accessories) clearly recognizable, just stylized in chibi form.
If the uploaded image is already a chibi / super-deformed / cartoon-style character:
Do not change the character’s face, facial expression, hairstyle, colors, or overall design.
Directly convert this exact design into a small cute 3D figure.
[SUBJECT]
small cute 3D figure style character based on the uploaded image,
big head, short body (2-head-tall chibi proportions),
toy-like look with realistic plastic texture,
single full-body character, centered in the frame

snow falling inside the globe,

random cute pose that fits the character’s personality

### 282. 电影级 AI 视频关键帧生成提示

**作者**: [松果先森](https://x.com/songguoxiansen/status/1996405859308781870)  **日期**: 2025-12-04  **语言**: zh

> 一个为 Nano Banana Pro 设计的详细系统提示，旨在将单个参考图像转换为连贯的电影短片序列，输出 9-10 个 AI 视频就绪的关键帧。它包含关于连续性、景深、色彩分级的严格规则，并要求对场景、主题、故事和电影制作方法进行结构化分解。

![电影级 AI 视频关键帧生成提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1765991042869_cjf0nh_G7Soe0baIAA0rHV.jpg)

```
<role>
You are an award-winning trailer director + cinematographer + storyboard artist. Your job: turn ONE reference image into a cohesive cinematic short sequence, then output AI-video-ready keyframes.
</role>

<input>
User provides: one reference image (image).
</input>

<non-negotiable rules - continuity & truthfulness>
1) First, analyze the full composition: identify ALL key subjects (person/group/vehicle/object/animal/props/environment elements) and describe spatial relationships and interactions (left/right/foreground/background, facing direction, what each is doing).
2) Do NOT guess real identities, exact real-world locations, or brand ownership. Stick to visible facts. Mood/atmosphere inference is allowed, but never present it as real-world truth.
3) Strict continuity across ALL shots: same subjects, same wardrobe/appearance, same environment, same time-of-day and lighting style. Only action, expression, blocking, framing, angle, and camera movement may change.
4) Depth of field must be realistic: deeper in wides, shallower in close-ups with natural bokeh. Keep ONE consistent cinematic color grade across the entire sequence.
5) Do NOT introduce new characters/objects not present in the reference image. If you need tension/conflict, imply it off-screen (shadow, sound, reflection, occlusion, gaze).
</non-negotiable rules - continuity & truthfulness>

<goal>
Expand the image into a 10–20 second cinematic clip with a clear theme and emotional progression (setup → build → turn → payoff).
The user will generate video clips from your keyframes and stitch them into a final sequence.
</goal>

<step 1 - scene breakdown>
Output (with clear subheadings):
- Subjects: list each key subject (A/B/C…), describe visible traits (wardrobe/material/form), relative positions, facing direction, action/state, and any interaction.
- Environment & Lighting: interior/exterior, spatial layout, background elements, ground/walls/materials, light direction & quality (hard/soft; key/fill/rim), implied time-of-day, 3–8 vibe keywords.
- Visual Anchors: list 3–6 visual traits that must stay constant across all shots (palette, signature prop, key light source, weather/fog/rain, grain/texture, background markers).
</step 1 - scene breakdown>

<step 2 - theme & story>
From the image, propose:
- Theme: one sentence.
- Logline: one restrained trailer-style sentence grounded in what the image can support.
- Emotional Arc: 4 beats (setup/build/turn/payoff), one line each.
</step 2 - theme & story>

<step 3 - cinematic approach>
Choose and explain your filmmaking approach (must include):
- Shot progression strategy: how you move from wide to close (or reverse) to serve the beats
- Camera movement plan: push/pull/pan/dolly/track/orbit/handheld micro-shake/gimbal—and WHY
- Lens & exposure suggestions: focal length range (18/24/35/50/85mm etc.), DoF tendency (shallow/medium/deep), shutter “feel” (
```

**Related**: [[室内设计]]

### 284. Nano Banana Pro 撕纸风格切换编辑提示

**作者**: [てんねん](https://x.com/munou_ac/status/1996129537806213597)  **日期**: 2025-12-03  **语言**: en

> 一个详细的 Nano Banana Pro 图像编辑提示，用于添加水平撕纸条，其内部可以在线条艺术、水墨画、人物渲染、彩铅、水彩或铅笔画风格之间切换，同时保留原始角色和场景。

![Nano Banana Pro 撕纸风格切换编辑提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1764909252272_9wbhhd_G7OpzpjbAAArAAS.jpg)
![Nano Banana Pro 撕纸风格切换编辑提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1764909263804_ixlq43_G7Op-C-bgAEuLoh.jpg)
![Nano Banana Pro 撕纸风格切换编辑提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1764909266159_7uv4sl_G7Op_5tboAAB-eW.jpg)
![Nano Banana Pro 撕纸风格切换编辑提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1764909269212_kro3sp_G7OqBr5bUAAGeIs.jpg)

```
task: "edit-image: add widened torn-paper layered effect"

base_image:
  use_reference_image: true
  preserve_everything:
    - character identity
    - facial features and expression
    - hairstyle and anatomy
    - outfit design and colors
    - background, lighting, composition
    - overall art style

rules:
  - Only modify the torn-paper interior areas.
  - Do not change pose, anatomy, proportions, clothing details, shading, or scene elements.

effects:
  - effect: "torn-paper-reveal"
    placement: "across chest height"
    description:
      - Add a wide, natural horizontal tear across the chest area.
      - The torn interior uses the style defined in `interior_style`.

  - effect: "torn-paper-reveal"
    placement: "lower abdomen height"
    description:
      - Add a wide horizontal tear across the lower abdomen.
      - The torn interior uses the style defined in `interior_style`.

interior_style:
  mode: {argument name="画風モード" default="line-art"}

  style_settings:
    line-art:
      palette: "monochrome"
      line_quality: "clean, crisp"
      paper: "notebook paper with subtle ruled lines"

    sumi-e:
      palette: "black ink tones"
      brush_texture: "soft bleeding edges"
      paper: "plain textured paper"

    figure-render:
      material: "PVC-like"
      shading: "semi-realistic highlights"
      paper: "plain smooth surface"

    colored-pencil:
      stroke_texture: "visible pencil grain"
      palette: "soft layered hues"
      paper: "rough sketchbook paper"

    watercolor:
      palette: "soft transparent pigments"
      blending: "smooth bleeding"
      edges: "soft contours"
      paper: "watercolor paper texture"

    pencil-drawing:
      graphite_texture: "visible pencil grain"
      shading: "smooth gradients"
      line_quality: "mixed sharp and soft"
      tone: "gray-scale"
      paper: "notebook paper with faint ruled lines"
```

**Related**: [[水彩]]、[[手绘素描]]、[[综合艺术]]

### 286. 能量场屏障视觉特效和姿势调整 YAML 提示

**作者**: [てんねん](https://x.com/munou_ac/status/1994567138384994796)  **日期**: 2025-11-29  **语言**: en

> 一个详细的 YAML Nano Banana Pro 提示词，用于将角色的姿势改为双臂前伸，并在双手前方添加同心八边形能量场屏障，同时保留所有原始角色和背景细节。

![能量场屏障视觉特效和姿势调整 YAML 提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1764577540773_v85176_G64gFJzbkAQpKL2.jpg)
![能量场屏障视觉特效和姿势调整 YAML 提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1764577543806_hhuvsz_G64gKH-bkAQsjS9.jpg)

```
task: "pose-and-barrier-vfx"

reference_image:
  keep_original: true

subject:
  keep_character_design: true

rules:
  - do not change the character’s face, expression, hairstyle, anatomy, or proportions
  - do not change outfit, colors, lineart, or art style
  - do not change background, composition, shading, or lighting
  - all modifications occur only through the defined steps

steps:

  - step: "pose-adjustment"
    action:
      - extend both arms forward toward the viewer
      - rotate both palms to face directly toward the camera
      - fingers naturally spread
    constraints:
      forbidden:
        - altering facial expression
        - modifying outfit
        - adding props or new items
        - introducing glow or VFX

  - step: "energy-barrier-vfx"
    vfx:
      type: "concentric-octagonal-barrier"
      placement: "in front of both palms"

      geometry:
        shape: "regular octagon"
        structure: "multiple concentric octagonal surfaces"
        alignment:
          - all surfaces share the same center
          - all surfaces are parallel to the camera plane
          - no curvature or spherical distortion
        forbidden:
          - outline-only shapes
          - hollow frames
          - hexagonal shapes
          - domed or warped surfaces

      surface:
        fill: "center-to-edge radial gradient"
        colors:
          center: "white-yellow"
          mid: "orange-gold"
          edge: "transparent orange"
        glow:
          - strong center luminosity
          - soft bloom
          - refractive shimmer
        opacity: "semi-transparent"

      layering:
        count: {argument name="number of barrier layers" default="8"}
        direction: "stacked forward"

  - step: "text-overlay"
    text:
      content: "Prompt by てんねん@ munou_ac"
      position: "bottom-left"
      font_color: "white"
      font_size: "small"
      opacity: "0.9"

composition:
  camera:
    angle: "frontal"
    distance: "medium shot"
    focus: "hands and barrier surface"
  lighting:
    keep_original: true
  placement:
    barrier_position: "centered between both palms"
    size: "large frontal barrier"
```

**Related**: [[手绘素描]]、[[综合艺术]]、[[综合动漫]]

### 288. 《鬼灭之刃》风格的动漫变形与毛笔书法

**作者**: [SSSS_CRYPTOMAN](https://x.com/SSSS_CRYPTOMAN/status/1991715253298819480)  **日期**: 2025-11-21  **语言**: en

> 一个全面的英文提示，可将上传的图像转换为具有大胆笔墨书法、火焰效果和传统图案背景的戏剧性日式动漫插画，同时保留原始主题。

![《鬼灭之刃》风格的动漫变形与毛笔书法](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1763886294661_eae4nn_G6P7y1rbgAAvypz.jpg)

```
Transform the user-uploaded image (photo or illustration) into a dramatic Japanese-inspired anime artwork. Always extract and use only the subject (the person) from the source image, and completely ignore or remove the original background. If the source is an illustration, repaint it in a refined anime style with beautiful Japanese-inspired three-dimensional shading, adding depth, gradients, and luminous highlights for a polished finish. If the source is a photo, reinterpret it as a realistic anime illustration, preserving natural skin, hair, and material textures, but applying painterly anime shading with strong depth. In all cases, redraw the subject in a powerful, dynamic, and energetic pose with a vivid and lively expression.  

Foreground Calligraphy: Add large Japanese brush-style calligraphy in the very front, layered above both the character and the background. Use exactly the Japanese characters provided by the user (Kanji, Katakana, or Hiragana). Render the characters faithfully, without altering, breaking, or stylizing them incorrectly. Do not translate or replace them. The calligraphy should be bold black ink with a glowing blurred white outline, surrounded by sumi ink splashes and scattered brush marks to convey motion and impact. The text content will be 「{argument name="前景テキスト1" default="炎柱"}」 and 「{argument name="前景テキスト2" default="煉獄杏寿郎"}」.  

Attribute Effect: Add the specified attribute effect ({argument name="属性" default="Fire"}) flowing dynamically with the character’s movement, drawn in a modern Ukiyo-e-inspired anime style with dramatic shapes, glowing highlights, particles, and energy trails.  

Background: Do not include the original photo background under any circumstances. Instead, fill the entire background with stylized Japanese patterns (Seigaiha waves, Asanoha hemp leaf, Kikkō tortoise shell, stylized clouds, etc.) combined with glowing elemental effects. Use deep navy, gold, and contrasting tones to create a luxurious Japanese atmosphere. Keep the background dark and patterned so the character, calligraphy, and attribute effects remain the primary focus.  

Overall: Always preserve the subject’s essential traits (hairstyle, outfit, facial features, body type) while enhancing impact, movement, and Japanese aesthetics through dynamic shading, expressive brush calligraphy, dramatic attribute effects, and traditional motifs.
```

**Related**: [[浮世绘与日本传统]]、[[水彩]]、[[手绘素描]]
